Proposals for changes/additions: 
• 
Customer data update DH-111 added paragraph "Transaction processing 
to be considered" and "Processing" and "Significant errors and consequences" 
added details to the section. Transaction data sent by the seller to the table 
clarifications and additions sections 8, 9 and 10 (Chapter 4.1) 
• 
Customer data update request JVH DH-112 added paragraph "Event 
to be taken into account in the processing" and a clarification to the point "Starts when" and 
"Significant errors and consequences" and event data additions to the table 
sections 8 and 9 (chapter 4.2) 
• 
Customer data update request 3 party DH-113 added paragraph "Transaction 
to be taken into account during processing and clarifications to "Significant errors and 
consequences" as well as additions to the event information table sections 7 and 8 (Chapter 4.3) 
• 
Notice of the new contract DH-311 clarifications under "Significant 
vRhetes and consequences". Sanoma event information in section 7 "Contact person" 
and 16 "Contact information" clarifications (Chapter 6.1) 
• 
Confirmation of the online agreement under DH-312 Sanoma event information 
8 "Contact person" clarifications (Chapter 6.2)

things to consider in processing" and Sanoma's event information in section 10 
contact information and details on section 14 "Contact information" (Chapter 6.3)

things to consider in processing" and Sanoma's event information in section 9

29/09/2023 
preliminary 2.2 
2.2 version changes to functionality: 
• 
Location status update "Disabled" or "Removed from system" -
change to the space is not allowed if the place of use has a parallel place of use 
at the time of entry into force or thereafter. Also added focus 
from the moment of entry into force also to the corresponding rules concerning the energy community (already 
existing rules). (Chapters 4.7 and 4.8) Development Proposal #201 
• 
If the DH-341 process returns the effective previous/future vendor 
agreement, the DH-341-3 message conveys the reinstated agreement 
identifier (chapter 6.9.1). Development proposal #56 
o 
Update 17 October 2023: Contract ID in DH-341-3 message 
is also sent to the seller of the reinstated contract.  
• 
Added a new reason code 'Termination of the seller's activity' (AN05) for the contract 
for deciding. The seller can use the code when announcing the decision himself DH-
at the 331 event. If the operator uses the mass event for its operations 
for concluding sales contracts/future sales contracts of the finalizing seller 
for cancellation, the distribution system operator is notified of the terminations DH-331-2-
with messages and about cancellations with DH-341-2 messages. Regarding decisions 
messages (DH-331-2) use the new reason code AN05 and cancellation 
in messages concerning reason code AR02 ('The seller has canceled the contract'). 
(Chapters 6.6, 6.9.1, 6.10, 13.3.6, 13.3.10, 14) Development proposal #141  
• 
The balance sheet is attached to the seller at the time of connection, even without the seller 
connection request, if the previous disconnection is not related to the seller's request (chapter 7.2). 
Development proposal #183 
6/7/2023 
2.1 
2.1 version changes to functionality: 
• 
Termination and cancellation of the sales contract will be notified 
to the distribution system operator also when there is a network contract corresponding to the sales contract 
unconfirmed (chapters 6.6 and 6.9.1). Development proposal #41

Changes 
• 
Restricted authorizations allowed for the seller, 3rd party and distribution system operator 
purposes (distribution system operator is not allowed to be authorized by any current 
on purpose) (Chapters 11.1 and 11.2). Development proposal #65 
• 
Deleted rule "The contract to be concluded must be valid at the time of notification" 
From the DH-333 incident (Chapter 6.8). Development proposal #70 
• 
In reasoning about the need for a new network contract, an 'electricity supply contract'-
based on the information, the existing online agreement is also taken into account (chap 
6.1). Development proposal #144 
• 
The balance sheet information is attached back to the seller in connection with the connection request, if 
the connection request is reported on the same day as the previous disconnection request (chap 
7.1). Development proposal #182 
• 
It is also possible to update the structural information of the product 
tax rate information of the product component (chapter 10.4). Development proposal #9, implemented already 
to version 2.0. 
Other updates: 
• 
Added a rule that was missing from the description, according to which measurement data cannot be used 
deliver to the under-construction measuring point (chapter 5.1).  
• 
Corrected searches for metering, netting calculation and energy community calculation data 
interval rule description. The search period can be a maximum of 7 days, 
when the search is made for the entire measurement area. Added recommendation that the measurement points 
the maximum number in the search is 1000 measurement points when the search is made for individuals 
for measurement points. (Chapters 5.2, 5.5, 5.7) 
• 
Added clarification on the use of the measurement point type for measurement, netting calculation and 
in searches for energy community calculation data, when searching in invoicing 
information to be used (chapters 5.2, 5.5, 5.7 and 13.3.14). 
• 
Corrected the description of the rules regarding consumption and small production locations 
belonging to the energy community (chapters 4.11 and 4.12). 
• 
Added a rule missing from the description, according to which the energy community 
the share of the member's place of use cannot be 100% (chapters 4.18 and 4.19). 
• 
Added missing items in the description of the sales contract update (DH-321). 
validation rules regarding timeliness (chapter 6.3). 
• 
Added note that transaction DH-344 should not be used. Belongs to 
to development proposal #121. (Chapter 6.9.4) 
• 
Corrected description of the information used in the message, if there is an online agreement 
cancellation of termination (DH-352) follows the cancellation of the sales contract termination (DH-351) (chapter 6.11). 
• 
Removed incorrect examples (P1D, P1M, P1Y) of the measurement time step from message E58 (chapter 13.3.4). 
• 
Corrected the DH-143 process entry date (energy community termination date) in message F26 (chapter 13.3.7). 
• 
Removed incorrect transaction ID ending (-1) from transactions DH-
141/142/143 (chapters 2.8.1, 2.8.2, 4, Appendix A). 
• 
Added to the image the missing messages DH-112-3/4/5, DH-
113-3, DH-122-4/5 & DH-820 from DH-100 events and the missing event ID endings 
(-1) for events DH-131/132/133/134/135 (chapter 4).

DH-331-4/5/6, DH-333-3, DH-341-4, DH-351-4/5, DH-352-3 & DH-820 from DH-300 events (chapter 6).

Changes 
• 
Updated the name of the billing channel AI05 from Netposti to OmaPosti (entire 
document). 
• 
Removed an incorrect example of using a wildcard in the 
declaration of the point of use ID (section 2.7). 
• 
Added a rule to the description of the DH-810 process that the point of use must not be 
deleted or deactivated (section 11.1). 
15.7.2022 
1.13 
• 
Changes to the message header in section 13.1: 
o 
The length of the field Message number <MessageNumber> has been changed from 4 to 
6 and the example from 0 to 1. 
o 
The length of the field Total messages <MessagesTotal> has been changed from 4 to 
6. 
• 
Added section 2.16 for assignments. 
• 
Added description of process validations in section 2.5.2. 
• 
Updated rules related to the type of customer identifier in sections 4.1, 4.2, 4.3, 
6.1.1 and 6.7. The party's own identifier is also allowed for corporate customers. 
• 
Added information that updated customer information is also forwarded to a seller whose 
contract has ended no more than 6 weeks earlier (chapter 4.1). 
• 
Added information that DH-112 is accepted with unchanged information if 
it is a response to an update request (chapter 4.2). 
• 
Added DH-122-2 message to the seller of a parallel usage point if 
the creation or update of a usage point involves a parallel usage point 
and a rule that parallel usage points belong to the same 
metering area (chapters 4.6 and 4.7). 
• 
Removed role Z08 from examples (chapter 13.2). 
• 
Added information that DH-132 does not return network agreement information if 
the network agreement corresponding to the sales agreement has not yet been confirmed (chapter 
4.11). 
• 
Clarified in the text that two move-in agreements cannot be reported for the same 
start date (the latter will be rejected) (chapter 6.1). 
• 
Clarified in the text that the 14-day time limit does not apply to 
seller exchange agreements if the previous sales agreement has already ended (chapter 
6.1). 
• 
Added rules regarding the end date of the agreement in the DH-311 event 
(chapter 6.1): 
o 
The end date is required in the case where the corresponding 
network agreement has been reported to be terminated. 
o 
The end date can be reported up to 90 days in the future. 
• 
Added to the description of creating a network agreement a situation where a new

1 
Introduction 
1.1 
General 
This document contains the interface descriptions related to the data exchange of the data hub. Document 
is based on datahub's business processes and data model. 
The documentation has been produced in close cooperation with the industry and datahub's technical department 
by a group of experts. The industry was also given the opportunity to comment on the document 
after its completion.  
Chapter 2 presents general rules related to messages and events that apply to interfaces 
generally.  
Chapters 4-12 describe the information content used in different datahub events, events 
intermediary chains and preliminary transaction validations. 
The event validations presented in the document are preliminary and the validations will be refined 
in the planning and implementation phase of the system. In addition to the checks listed 
event validation checks event-specific data requirements and enumerations, i.e 
code lists. A negative acknowledgment is returned for incorrect transactions.  
Chapter 13 describes the general message types that are used to implement the events described in Chapters 4-12. 
The XML specifications will be made according to this chapter. 
 
 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

Fingrid Datahub Oy

firstname.surname@fingrid.fi

2 
General interface specifications 
ebIX® message specifications (www.ebix.org) are used as the basis for the interface specifications, 
the combined Nordic retail market (Harmonized Nordic Retail project / HNR) and Norway 
specifications and documentation of the datahub project (Elhub). 
The standards and message definitions presented above have been applied where possible. Finland 
however, the datahub's functional set is considerably wider, so the existing 
the direct utilization of the specifications as such remains limited. Finland compared to Elhub 
datahub models a centralized customer register, sales and 
online contract information, product and price information, and invoice line information. In addition, Finland's data hub 
is entirely based on hourly measurement data, while in Elhub it is also processed 
profile usage readings. Due to the reasons described above, we have had to use interfaces 
to make a significant number of national expansions. Because the number of plugins needed is 
significant, in certain situations the message structure is also simplified compared to ebIX-
to message specifications. 
The acknowledgment message that uses the ebIX structure, which is defined, is used as the acknowledgment message 
for the datahub's needs.  
2.1 
Namespace (namespace)  
The XML namespace is used to identify the elements and attributes of messages and events. Datahub-
the namespace definition is used in messages: 
urn:fi:datahub:mif:<Package>:<Message type>_<Message name>:<Major version> 
Package - The following values ​​are used: 
• 
masterdata - Messages related to structural data updates 
• 
metering - Messages related to metering data 
• 
invoicing- Messages related to invoicing 
• 
query - Messages related to queries 
• 
common - The namespace of the common elements of the messages. 
Message type defines the type of message. 
• 
E.g. F01 
Message name defines the name of the message. 
• 
E.g. MasterDataCustomerEvent

Major version specifies the message version, the prefix v is used. 
Example: 
<xmlns:rsm="urn:fi:Datahub:mif:invoicing:F13_InvoicingDataInfo:v1"> 
 
Namespaces to be used are described in more detail in Datahub's XML schema specification. 
2.2 
Versioning 
2.2.1 
Newspaper version 
The message version is represented in the namespace definitions of the xml file. There will be a news version 
to update in a situation where changes are made to messages that do not backfire anymore 
compatibility with the previous message version. Such changes include, for example: 
• 
Deleting or changing enumeration values 
• 
Changes to the names of elements, types, or attributes 
• 
Changes to the structure or order of the message 
• 
Removing or adding required elements or attributes 
• 
Making elements or attributes mandatory 
2.2.2 
A subversion of Sanoma 
Message definitions can be updated with a subversion without a version update when the messages 
backward compatibility is maintained. These changes are represented in the XML schema definition 
with the xsd:version attribute in the schema file (.xsd). 
• 
Adding enumeration values 
• 
Optional message extensions  
2.3 
Message structure 
All datahub messages consist of the following parts: 
• 
Message header information 
• 
Process information 
• 
eventum data

Note: 
Focusing 
[1] 
In Datahub's message traffic, all received messages are created 
acknowledgment message. The acknowledgment request is not presented in the message header. 
[2] 
The message identifier must always be unique for each sender. Datahub rejects the message if 
a message with the same message ID has already been received from the same sender and it is 
asynchronous event (see chapter 2.12 of this document and Datahub External Interface 
Specification). The retransmission is always done with a new message ID and to corrected ones 
for information and also in a situation where the same information is sent again. 
[3] 
The technical operator of the message means the party that delivers/receives the message. 
The legal operator of the message refers to the party whose information is processed in the message. 
For example, if the service provider takes care of the measurement data collection and delivery to the data hub 
(on behalf of the distribution system operator), the technical sender is the service provider and the legal sender is 
distribution system operator. The technical operator must always have the authorization of the legal operator in question 
to the process. 
[4] 
The sender of the message can set the routing information in the message, which is returned in the acknowledgment message. 
The routing information can be used in the routing of the received acknowledgment to the original one 
to the system that sent the message. 
[5] 
In Datahub's processes, DH-22* responses can contain such a large amount of information that it 
it makes sense to split into several different messages so that the size of one message does not grow huge. 
In this case, the fields Message number and Total messages are filled with numbers that indicate 
how many different messages the information content is divided into and which message from the series is in question.

2.4.2 
Parties and measurement areas 
GLN codes from the GS1 system are used for party identifiers, and for measurement areas 
Y codes of the EIC code set. 
2.4.3 
Location IDs 
GSRN codes from the GS1 system are used for place of use codes. 
2.4.4 
Timestamps and time intervals 
All timestamps are presented in UTC (Coordinated Universal Time) and in XML format YYYY-
MM-DDTHH:MM:SS+00:00 or YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ. 
Example: 
2015-06-12T21:00:00+00:00 
2015-06-12T21:00:00Z 
By default, the validity periods (start time and end time) are set to the limit of a day (Finland 
official time). In measurement data, time stamps are set to full hours. Message creation times (and 
other similar technical event times) are presented with an accuracy of one second.

The expiration dates of the terms of validity (e.g. the end date of the agreement) are presented 
at the time of termination. For example, if the contract expires on December 31, 2015, 
the end time is 2015-12-31T22:00:00+00:00 (in Finnish official time the time 
01.01.2016 00:00). 
Some time limits in this document are specified in years. In Datahub, a year means 365 
days. 
2.4.5 
Units of values 
The SI system codes are used as unit codes for the values, e.g. kW, MW, kWh, 
MWh, kvar, Mvar, kvarh, Mvarh. 
2.4.6 
Message IDs 
UUIDs (Universally Unique Identifiers) are used as identifiers for messages. 
2.5 
Message validations 
Datahub validates messages at the three levels shown below. 
2.5.1 
XML schema 
In XML schema validation, the message is checked against the schema on a technical level. Validation 
checks the mandatory and data format of the message structure, elements and attributes 
correctness (format and maximum field length) and data enumerations. In the event of an error 
a SOAP level rejection (SOAP Fault) is returned. 
2.5.2 
Process validations 
In process validation, the process level information, the process ID and role, and the party are checked 
rights to report that process event. Datahub checks the sender of the message 
user rights on two different levels: the notifier's right to initiate said market event (eg 
DH-131) and the notifier's right to market information related to the message (such as a specific place of use).  
The right to the processed market data is always checked solely on the basis of the legal sender. 
The right to perform a certain market transaction is also based on the user rights of the legal sender 
(the right is determined through the market role). However, the legal sender can give to another person 
the party the right to notify a certain event on its own behalf. In this case, you must go to the data hub 
defined as the so-called assignment, which is described in chapter 2.16. 
The allowed roles of message senders are listed in the paragraph Sanomalist. In the event of an error 
a SOAP fault (SOAP Fault) is returned.

2.5.3 
Event validations 
Transaction validation includes transaction-specific validations in accordance with the market process, which do not 
Validate in XML schema and process validations. Validation is performed in event validation 
fulfillment of dependencies and time limits between the attributes of the notification. In addition, declared values 
is validated against the data content of the data hub. The validations for the passed transaction are returned 
positive acknowledgment message. Incorrect messages will be returned with a negative acknowledgement 
error message (error code and error text). 
In connection with event validation, the values ​​of the declared attributes are also validated according to the data standard 
against the rules defined in the "allowed values" column. A Finnish personal identification number will be required 
for example, fulfills the requirements set for it by legislation 
(http://www.finlex.fi/fi/laki/ajantasa/2010/20100128). 
The event-specific descriptions (chapters 4-12) list those related to the event in question 
event validations. 
2.6 
Receipt processing 
Datahub acknowledges the parties' requests on two different levels: on the technical level and on the process level. 
On a technical level, the datahub interface always responds to each party's request, indicating whether 
request understoodretted and received in full or not. This is the so-called interface technical 
acknowledgment, which is separate from, for example, the business so-called presented in sequence diagrams 
process level acknowledgements. These technical acknowledgments are not modeled in sequence diagrams.  
Datahub always delivers either a positive or negative acknowledgment to received messages 
also at the process level. The information returned in survey events serves as a positive acknowledgment 
and a negative acknowledgment message is returned from the error situation. In negative acknowledgment 
the errors manifested in the process and event validation described in chapter 2.5 are reported. 
For synchronous services, process-level acknowledgment is returned to the party after 
datahub has fully processed the service request. For asynchronous services 
datahub first returns a technical acknowledgment of the approval of the request and later 
of processing the asynchronous process-level acknowledgment event itself. Asynchronous services and 
their acknowledgment processes are described in more detail in chapter 2.12. Always used in the Datahub interface 
acknowledgment message in such a way that the header information of the message does not specify separately whether acknowledgment is desired 
or not. 
When retrieving messages from the data hub, the receiving party must acknowledge receipt of the messages 
as described in chapter 2.11. 
In the Datahub interface, process-level acknowledgments comply with the ebIX structure 
an acknowledgment message containing a header, process and acknowledgment event. Sanoma's process section 
has the same content as in the original message to be acknowledged. The content of the acknowledgment event is 
next.

2.10 
Mediation of events 
Datahub forwards the received events to the necessary parties. Forwarded by default 
the same information as in the received message. If the information content differs, it is mentioned separately. 
For contract events (contract creation and update events), separate ones have been defined 
transmission transactions, because not all contractual information should be transmitted between the parties. 
If the update event notified to datahub based on the update request does not already contain changes 
compared to the information in the datahub, the information is forwarded only to the party that is 
requested information update. Such request events include a request to update customer information 
from the distribution system operator to the seller and a request to update the usage location information from the seller to the distribution system operator. 
2.11 
Event pickup 
Datahub does not deliver messages to the parties automatically, instead the messages are buffered 
to the transmission queue, from which the party retrieves the messages one at a time. Datahub delivers the messages 
in the order according to the creation time shown in the message header information. The retrieved message remains 
still available for pickup by the party until the party has separately notified datahub 
having received the message. The parties retrieve the messages using a retrieval event.  
The information content of the pick-up event is as follows: 
Data field 
Level 
Obligation 
Comment 
Note: 
Pickup event 
1 
1..1

Asynchronous searches, i.e. searches for measurement data and calculation line data, are differentiated on each side 
into their own separate queues. In this case, asynchronous searches do not mix with other information exchange. 
The measurement data is broken down for each party separately by datahub in transaction DH-211 
and to the queues of measurement data requested by the party with DH-220 transactions. The parties can decide themselves 
how the queues will be unloaded into the party's own systems when implementing the interface. 
2.12 
Synchronicity/asynchrony of events 
In terms of structural data update and query events, the service interfaces are synchronous. 
Acknowledgment and/or response information to the survey is returned as a response to the service request of the same session 
during. 
In terms of time series data (measurement data and balance sheet information) and invoice line data, the services are 
asynchronous for both notification events and search events. Datahub restores 
immediately a synchronous technical level acknowledgment that the party's request/notification is 
accepted for processing. Acknowledgments of the actual transaction processing and response information to the survey 
returned separately via the pick-up service asynchronously. 
2.12.1 Asynchronous searches 
When a search event arrives, the interface checks that the search is in the form of specifications 
adequate. At the same time, a check is made that the party has the right to send based on its role 
that kind of search event. If the form check or role check produces a negative result, 
datahub returns a negative acknowledgment and the processing of the search ends. 
If the application transaction is in the correct format, and the party has the necessary role for the transaction, 
datahub starts processing the search. In this context, we check whether the party has the right 
to the requested information at the point of use level. If the party has applied for a wider set of data, from which 
he is only entitled to a part, datahub returns the part of the requested data to which the party is a party 
is right. An error message will be returned for the information to which the applicant is not entitled.

2.13 
Encryption and compression of message traffic 
Transactions are transferred encrypted HTTPS (TLS 1.2). Messages are signed using certificates 
WS-Security. Messages are not separately encrypted using WS-Security. 
The measurement data events to be sent must be compressed, and the measurement data transmitted by the data hub must be compressed accordingly 
the events are packed. Compression is done during data transfer (HTTP/S) using HTTP 
Compression technology. 
2.14 
The ID and sender of the original message 
Several datahub transactions have the information field "Identifier of the original message". This field 
is used to link related events into a chain of events. The field is not used in the chain 
in the first events, but in the other events of the event chain this field is always 
the message ID of the previous event. 
Example:  
1. The seller announces the new contract with transaction DH-311-1. Not used in this event 
"Identifier of the original message" field, because it starts the chain 
2. Datahub transmits information about the new contract to the distribution system operator with transaction DH-311-
2. In this transaction, the field contains the message ID of the previous DH-311-1 transaction.

3. The distribution network operator confirms the network contract with transaction DH-312-1. Since the event

the field contains the message ID of the previous DH-311-2 event. 
4. Datahub transmits information about the confirmation of the online contract to the seller with transaction DH-312-2. 
In this transaction, the field contains the message ID of the previous DH-312-1 transaction. 
The sender data field of the original message is used accordingly. In the example described above 
in transaction DH-311-2, the field would indicate that the original DH-311-1 transaction was sent 
seller ID. In event DH-312-1, the sender of event DH-311-2 is indicated in the field (i.e 
data hub). In transaction DH-312-2, the field states that transaction DH-312-1 has been sent 
ID of the distribution system operator. 
2.15 
Structural data updates 
In Datahub, structural data updates are processed in two alternative ways: 
as a full update or a partial update.  
Size update is used for all structural data updates other than 
in updating customer information. For example, updating the usage location information updates all the reported ones 
information. When the distribution system operator updates the data of the point of use, the previously valid data of the point of use 
the information will cease to be valid and will be replaced by new information provided. If so 
for example, previously there were 6 addresses in the place of use, but in the update there are only 4 in the place of use 
address, in the future only the 4 addresses indicated in the update will be valid in the datahub at the place of use. 
In a partial update, only the information indicated in the event is updated. Partial update is used 
of actual update events only when updating customer data. If customer data 
in the update, in addition to the mandatory information, only the customer's e-mail address is indicated, 
only the email address is updated in the customer's information. If the customer has already had 
phone number, it will not be deleted. If you want to delete some information from the data hub in the partial update, 
the data field in question is included in the event but empty. Data fields that partial update 
are not involved in the event retain their former value.  
Also in update request events (such as distribution system operator or 3rd party customer data 
update request, request to update user location information of the seller or a 3rd party) is used the same 
principle than in partial updates. Based on the request, the party making the actual update 
should interpret the received update request as a partial update. 
2.16 
Assignments 
The seller or the distribution system operator can commission another party (the seller, the distribution system operator or 
of a 3rd party) to announce datahub events or to pick up datahub's forwarded/announced events 
messages in turn. The assignment of notification messages means the assignment of a process (for example 
DH-311-1 Notice of new sales contract) initiated by the other party 
commissioned. The assignment of relay messages means that normally 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

Fingrid Datahub Oy

the message received by the principal is forwarded to the assignee instead of the principal 
(for example DH-111-2 Transmission of customer data to the distribution system operator). 
In assignments, the authorization to use the market data to be processed is carried out by the assignee 
according to the party's rights. More precisely, with regard to market data, the right of use check 
is performed in datahub according to the legal sender indicated in the market message (see 2.16.1). 
The assignment of notification and forwarding messages can be applied separately to different parties 
regardless of the market event. In other words, the notification message of the same market event and 
proxy messages can be assigned to different parties (if in the said process the notifying party also 
receive relay messages). 
Each market transaction/broker message order between two parties 
is assigned to the datahub separately via the datahub user interface. This can only be done 
datahub operator. The operator adds orders from the ordering party's service request, 
which should be done through the support portal. Configurations are made in the datahub individually at the message level and 
the parties can search and view (but not update) assignments in the datahub user interface 
through. 
The assignments apply to both synchronous and asynchronous messages. 
2.16.1 Notification of the event by assignment 
The assignment of the market process entitles the contracting party to send B2B messages 
datahub on behalf of the commissioning party. This can be provided by the contracting party 
the right to several different contractors per market event.  
In a notification based on an assignment, the contracting party sends a message to datahub. 
In this case, the physical sender field of the message must contain the ID of the party who commissioned the order, and 
the legal sender field must contain the ID of the ordering party. The process role comes 
determine the message according to the legal party (for example, in DH-311 transactions 
the process role is "DDQ" i.e. Seller and not "THP" i.e. 3rd party). 
In the measurement data notification (DH-211) event, the commissioning party can also notify 
that they want a copy (CC) of the forwarding message. In this case, a proxy message is also formed 
to the ordering party's message queue. 
2.16.2 Assignment of a proxy message 
The forwarding message assignment defines which forwarding messages are sent to the contractor 
instead of the ordering party. 
In mandated forwarding messages, the physical recipient field has the assignee 
the party's ID, and the legal recipient field contains the assigning party's ID. So 
in age forwarding messages, the process role corresponds to the legal one according to the transaction definition 
the role of the receiver.

to the physical sender of the message.  
The copy (CC) option for mandated relay messages is not currently defined 
to any of the current market events and it is thus not possible for the time being. 
In assignments of relay messages, all messages related to the same process (can be several 
notifications) are assigned to one (and therefore the same) organization. 
2.16.3 General rules for assignments 
The following principles apply to the commissioning of processes (market events): 
• 
Announcements or proxy messages where the market/process role is "3rd party" are not allowed 
commission. 
• 
In searches for measurement, balance sheet, product, and invoice line data, a query message can be used 
commissions and the requested information is always returned to the physical person who initiated the transaction 
to the sender.

3 
Descriptions of Datahub events 
The following chapters describe datahub events, their rules and data contents. In this chapter 
The operation of datahub events is described in general, and future chapters are presented 
the structure of event descriptions. 
Datahub will be built on the basis of various events (services). The event is 
a single interaction between the parties and datahub, usually a request, notification or information 
an update event consisting of the steps shown in the image below. 
 
FIGURE 111 DESCRIPTION OF THE PERFORMANCE OF THE DATAHUB EVENT 
1. The party initiates the transaction by making a change to its own system, from which 
a transaction request is sent to the datahub interface. The request must contain the necessary information 
to complete the transaction. Datahub can also initiate the event. 
2. Datahub validates the format, data content and 
event-specific other rules. If validation fails, the transaction is aborted and 
the flow of the event moves to step 5. The levels of validation are described in more detail 
in the next chapter. 
3. If necessary, datahub processes data according to the definition of the event (for example 
different calculations). 
4. Data that is validated and generated or updated during possible processing is saved 
to the datahub database.

5. The party initiating the transaction will be acknowledged the success of the transaction or 
failure. After the rejecting acknowledgment, the party must correct the error and send 
request again. 
6. After successful execution, information is forwarded to a possible other party 
according to the specifications. The other party may send a new request 
based on the information it receives, resulting from the original event 
a chain of several events, i.e. a process.

such as seller–change or moving processes. Most of the events will start 
automatically when the party updates the information in its own system. Each party 
the responsibility is to put the information in the format required by datahub. 
After the table describing the execution of the event, a sequence diagram for the event is presented 
the related information exchange between the parties and the contents of the events as a class diagram. Class diagram 
a description of the message content of the event follows the tablein full size. The purpose of class diagrams is 
only represent what information is announced or conveyed in the event, it is not their purpose 
in its structure, it perfectly corresponds to the message description of the document. The messages will be implemented 
According to the Datahub events document.  
3.1 
Event cancellation and error correction 
Incorrectly reported data must be able to be corrected in datahub. The most important thing is that you don't stay in the data hub 
incorrect information for any period. Data correction is done in a different way, depending on what needs to be corrected 
about the event. 
A separate cancellation notification is used for the creation of a place of use, the seller's disconnection or connection request 
as well as in cancellations of the start or termination of the contract. In all measurement, use place, 
in updates of customer, product and invoice line information, as well as disconnections of the distribution network operator 
Incorrect information reported in connection notifications is corrected with new update events and not separately 
cancel. The corrected data must then be reported within the time limits of the market processes 
allowing at the same effective time that the incorrect information was originally sent, lest 
incorrect information remains in datahub. If there is no corrective update due to business rules 
possible to do at the same time of entry into force as the incorrect update, the correctors will be notified 
information on the effective date as early as the processes allow. 
In the case of cancellations, problems arise in situations where, based on incorrect information, there has already been time 
start other events. The main rule is that transactions at the place of use can only be canceled if 
There have been no other updates for the location in question since the original announcement 
by the parties. More detailed cancellation rules are described in the event descriptions.  
3.2 
Explanations of process maps 
In the process maps attached to the event descriptions, each event is summarized 
the process part contains. On the map, the events are not in their execution order, but that 
is described in chapter 3 of the document "Business processes of the electricity retail market".

4.1 
DH-111 Customer data update - seller 
TABLE 222 DESCRIPTION OF UPDATE OF CUSTOMER DATA BY SELLER 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller updates the customer's information in the datahub or responds to the customer's information 
to the update request. In response to a request to update customer information, it can be reported 
also valid customer information, which means that the update request has been rejected. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution Network Operator (Network Service Provider), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer has notified the seller of the change in information, who updates the information with his own 
information system, or the seller has received a request to update customer information 
from datahub. 
Information to be reported 
Customer information; name, address, name/date of birth, y-identification number or personal identification number of the party, 
language code, contact information (e-mail, phone number, official postal address). 
The date when the changed information becomes effective, optional legend 
about the update. 
The event 
processing 
worth noting 
Customer data updates should not be automatically sent to any data hub 
an event forwarded to the party, such as, for example, a request to update customer information 
(DH-112-2/DH-113-2) basis.  
The update must be based on the customer's verified need for change 
Updates to customer information made by the party in its own system will not be included 
sends an update message if the update does not change those maintained in the data hub 
customer information. 
Updating customer data should not automatically trigger another event, such as 
for example, updating the billing address of the contract (DH-321), if the information is not there 
changed in that regard as well. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have a sales contract with the customer, which is either valid 
at the announced update effective time, comes into effect at the announced update time 
after or has ended no more than 6 weeks before the update is notified to datahub. 
Code 
The customer must be found in the data hub. 
The customer type cannot be changed. 
An encrypted client cannot be upgraded to non-encrypted with this transaction. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The customer's updated information is taken to datahub immediately when it is the seller's 
system updated 
The effective date must not be in the past and can be no more than the 90th 
days in the future. Valid periods are whole days.  
When the seller responds to the customer information update request, the update must be sent by two 
within one business day of receiving the update request. The update is accepted 
even later, but notifications sent repeatedly late will be addressed 
to intervene. 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

Processing 
If the client becomes secret, all client authorizations are terminated. 
When updating customer information, a partial update is used, where only the information entered in the transaction is updated. 
Data fields that are not included in the transaction retain their previous value. If desired in partial update 
deletes some data from the data hub, that data field will be included in the transaction as empty. 
For example, if in the update of the customer information, in addition to the mandatory information, only the customer is reported 
e-mail address, the e-mail address is updated from the customer's voluntary information. If the customer already has 
a previously saved phone number, for example, remains unchanged.   
Data storage 
Reported information 
The customer information provided by the seller takes effect on the announced effective date. 
Old data is stored in the data hub. The seller is primarily responsible for customer data 
of correctness. 
Processed data 
Any updated authorization information. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected update of customer information 
Transmission of information 
Alreadys update includes changes to customer information, customer information is forwarded to sellers and 
for distribution system operators who have a valid license at the time of entry into force or a maximum of 6 
expired a week earlier (only in the case of the seller) or will take effect in the future 
the future contract with the customer and for 3rd parties who have a valid 
authorization from the customer. 
If the event is a response to the distribution system operator's update request (DH-112), the information 
are forwarded to the distribution system operator who requested the update, even if they do not contain 
changes. 
If the customer is encrypted, the information contained in the update is never forwarded to 3rd parties. 
If the customer becomes secret, the notification of the change in authorization is forwarded to them 
to the parties whose authorizations were decided. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Incorrect customer information is forwarded to all parties who are entitled 
to customer information. 
Maintaining the correctness of the data is the responsibility of the personal data registrar. 
Passing on incorrect personal data is a violation of data protection. 
The customer's postal address is given incorrectly → Possible mails (incl. invoices) go 
to the wrong address, especially if the contract does not specify a separate one 
billing address. The result may be wrong collection actions or a data breach. 
The customer's contact information is reported incorrectly or incomplete → The customer cannot be reached 
contact, as the existing contact information will be deleted 
The customer's name information is reported incorrectly → Any mail (incl. invoices) will not go through 
arrive or go to the wrong recipient. 
Cancellation terms 
The cancellation is made with a new update notification. If the effective date is 
in the future, a message will be sent where has the same effective date as 
in the original message. If the effective date is in the past, 
the current day is used in the update notification.

[*] 
Datahub always forwards the customer's complete information, which is valid, to other parties 
at the time the update takes effect. If the update contains only part of the customer data, 
forwarding messages are supplemented with the customer's information already found in the data hub 
with customer information. If any customer information has been deleted in the update (sent element 
as empty), the element in question is missing from the notifications forwarded by datahub. 
See more Business processes of the electricity retail market in datahub chapter 3.1.2

If the message DH-111-1 is the answer DH-112 or DH-113 tashould be used in the field 
DH-112-2 or DH-113-2 message ID, respectively. When the datahub forwards the update to others 
for the parties (DH-111-2, DH-111-3 and DH-111-4), the field contains the ID of the DH-111-1 message. 
[2] 
If the party's own ID is used, it is of the form <seller's ID>_<customer number> 
(used as identifying information in a situation where the personal identification number is not known/y identification number is not available 
be).

4.2 
DH-112 Customer data update request - JVH 
TABLE 333 DESCRIPTION OF UPDATE OF CUSTOMER DATA BY DISTRIBUTION NETWORK OPERATOR 
THROUGH THE AGENCY OF 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator updates customer information in its own system, which it reports 
update request to datahub. The update request is forwarded last to the customer of the contract 
to the seller who made the deal with, who will make the actual update to the datahub because it is 
responsible for updating customer information to datahub. If the the customer does not have 
contracts other than the online contract in the datahub, the information is updated directly 
to the datahub based on the distribution system operator's notification. 
The parties and 
roles 
Distribution system operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer informs the distribution system operator of the change in information and the distribution system operator 
updates the information in its own system or it is a third-party response 
to the customer data update request sent by the party in a situation where 
the customer does not have a salesperson. 
Notifiable 
information 
Customer identifier, identifier type, customer type, date when 
the changed information comes into effect and a voluntary explanation of the update. In addition 
of the following information, those to which a change is desired (see the principle of partial updates 
in chapter 2.15): name, address, name/date of birth, y-identification number or the party's own identification number, 
language code, contact information (phone number, email address, official postal address). 
The event 
processing 
worth noting 
The customer data update request should not be sent automatically by any data hub 
an event communicated to the party, such as, for example, a notification of a new 
based on the sales contract (DH-311-2).  
The update request must be based on the customer's verified need for change. 
Updates to customer information made by the party in its own system will not be included 
sends an update request to the datahub if the update does not change those maintained in the datahub 
customer information. 
A customer data update request should not automatically cause another event, 
such as updating the contract's billing address (DH-322), if not the information 
haven't changed in that regard either. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The distribution system operator must have a contract with the customer, which is either valid 
at the announced update entry into force or comes into effect at the announced update entry point 
after. 
Code 
The customer can be found in datahub. 
The customer type cannot be changed. 
An encrypted client cannot be upgraded or requested to be upgraded to non-encrypted with this 
at the event. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
 
  
Datahub events

Time limits 
The customer's updated information is reported to the datahub immediately when it is available 
updated in the distribution system operator's system 
The effective date of the change must not be in the past and it can be no more than 90 
days in the future. Valid periods are whole days. 
Processing 
Datahub checks whether the information in the update request is the same as the valid customer information. If they are, 
a negative acknowledgment is returned, and no further actions are taken (unless it is a response 
to an update request, in which case unchanged data is also allowed). Otherwise 
datahub checks whether the customer has a sales contract (seller who has the right to customer data). If so, 
datahub does not store data, but forwards the data to the seller who has last done business with the customer 
contract. If not, datahub updates the information directly from the distribution system operator's notification. If datahub 
update the customer's information based on the distribution system operator's notification and the customer becomes secret, 
all client authorizations are terminated. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
Changed customer information and the change date, if the customer only has 
online contract. Old data is stored in the data hub. 
Processed 
information 
Any updated authorization information. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected update or transfer of customer information 
to the seller. If the customer does not have sales contracts in datahub, updated information 
is returned as confirmation to the distribution system operator that sent the notification. 
Transmission of information 
The update request is forwarded to the seller who was the last to sign the contract. 
with the customer.  
The transmitted information does not indicate from which party the update request originates. 
If the customer does not have a salesperson, the updated customer information is forwarded to the customer 
to possible other distribution system operators who have a valid or future one 
the contract with the customer coming into force, and to 3rd parties with authorization 
to the customer's information. 
If the authorizations were decided on the basis of a notice from the distribution system operator, the notice 
the change of authorization is communicated to the parties whose authorizations were decided. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant 
errors and 
consequences 
Incorrect customer information is forwarded to all parties who are entitled 
to customer information. 
Maintaining the correctness of the data is the responsibility of the personal data registrar. 
Passing on incorrect personal data is a violation of data protection. 
The customer's mailing address is reported incorrectly→ Possible mails (incl. invoices) go 
to the wrong address, especially if the contract does not specify a separate one 
billing address. The result may be wrong collection actions or a data breach. 
The customer's contact information is reported incorrectly or incomplete → The customer cannot be reached 
contact, as the existing contact information will be deleted 
The customer's name information is reported incorrectly → Any mail (incl. invoices) will not go through 
arrive or go to the wrong recipient. 
Cancellation terms 
-

4.3 
DH-113 Customer data update request - 3rd party 
TABLE 444 DESCRIPTION OF UPDATE OF CUSTOMER INFORMATION BY A 3RD PARTY 
Event description 
Definition 
The 3rd party updates customer data in its own system, which it reports 
update request to datahub. The update request is forwarded last to the customer of the contract 
to the seller who made the deal with, who makes the actual update to the data hub, because it is 
responsible for updating customer information to datahub. If the the customer does not have 
contracts other than the network contract in the datahub, the update request is forwarded last 
to the distribution network operator who has concluded the contract with the customer. Here 
the distribution system operator can update the customer information in the data hub with its own update request 
(DH-112). 
The parties and 
roles 
3rd party (Energy service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), Distribution system operator 
(Network service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer informs the 3rd party of the data change and the 3rd party updates the information 
to its own system 
Notifiable 
information 
Customer identifier, identifier type, customer type, date when 
the changed information comes into effect and a voluntary explanation of the update. In addition 
of the following information, those to which a change is desired (see the principle of partial updates 
in chapter 2.15): name, address, surname/date of birth or social security number, language code, contact information 
(phone number, e-mail address, official postal address). 
The event 
processing 
worth noting 
The customer data update request should not be sent automatically by any data hub 
the event forwarded to the party, such as the customer information of the notification 
based on the update (DH-111-4).  
The update request must be based on the customer's verified need for change. 
Updates to customer information made by the party in its own system will not be included 
sends an update request to the datahub if the update does not change those maintained in the datahub 
customer information. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The 3rd party must be authorized to update the customer's information 
at the time of entry into force. 
Code 
The customer can be found in datahub. 
The customer type cannot be changed. 
The customer must have a valid sales or online contract at the time of notification 
at some point of use in the data hub. 
An encrypted client cannot be requested to be upgraded to non-encrypted with this transaction. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The customer's updated information is reported to datahub immediately when it is from a 3rd party 
system updated. 
The effective date of the change must not be in the past and it can be no more than 90 
days in the future. Valid periods are whole days. 
Processing

Datahub checks whether the information in the update request is the same as the valid customer information. If they are, 
a negative acknowledgment is returned and no further action is taken. Otherwise, datahub checks, 
does the customer have a sales contract (seller who has the right to customer data). If so, datahub cares 
information for the seller who most recently entered into a sales contract with the customer. If not, we will care 
update request to the distribution system operator that has most recently entered into a network contract with the customer. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed 
information 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification successfulfrom sleep or from a rejected update request relay. 
Transmission of information 
The update request is forwarded to the seller who was the last to sign the contract. 
with the customer. If the customer does not have sales contracts in datahub, updated ones 
the information is forwarded to the distribution system operator, which was the last to conclude the contract. 
with the customer. 
The transmitted information does not indicate from which party the update request originates. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant 
errors and 
consequences 
Incorrect customer information is forwarded to all parties who are entitled 
to customer information. 
Maintaining the correctness of the data is the responsibility of the personal data registrar. 
Passing on incorrect personal data is a violation of data protection. 
The customer's postal address is given incorrectly → Possible mails (incl. invoices) go 
to the wrong address, especially if the contract does not specify a separate one 
billing address.  The result may be wrong collection actions or a data breach. 
The customer's contact information is reported incorrectly or incomplete → The customer cannot be reached 
contact, as the existing contact information will be deleted 
The customer's name information is reported incorrectly → Any mail (incl. invoices) will not go through 
arrive or go to the wrong recipient. 
Cancellation terms 
-

DH-114 Notification of updating the customer's identifier 
TABLE 555 DESCRIPTION OF CUSTOMER ID UPDATE NOTICE 
Event description 
Definition 
The Datahub operator updates the customer's identifier. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution Network Operator (Network Service Provider), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The Datahub operator has been asked to update the customer's identifier. 
Information to be reported 
The customer's new and old identifier, the effective date of the change, other up-to-date information 
customer information. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
Notification of the update is sent to sellers who have at the time of notification of the update 
valid, coming into force in the future or expired less than 6 weeks ago 
sales contract with the customer. 
Notification of the update is sent to distribution system operators who have the update 
the online contract valid at the time of notification or coming into force in the future 
with the customer. 
Notification of the update is sent to 3rd parties who have the update at the time of notification 
valid or future authorization for the customer's data. 
Code 
In the event, only the customer's identifier is updated, not other customer information. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
The customer's new identifier. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
- 
Transmission of information 
According to the rights described above, new and old identification, change 
the effective date as well as the valid customer information are forwarded to the customer's information 
to authorized sellers, distribution system operators and third parties. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The wrong identifier is updated for the customer -> The customer cannot access his data 
through the customer portal. The customer can be in the data hub with two different IDs. 
Cancellation terms 
The cancellation is made with a new update notification.

4.5 
DH-116 Connecting customers 
TABLE 666 DESCRIPTION OF CUSTOMER COMBINATION 
Event description 
Definition 
Customer integration prosessi is triggered when a market participant tries to update 
from the customer identification party's own ID (AA04) to a personal identification number 
(AA03) and the update is rejected because there is already one with the specified ID 
customer in datahub. 
In this case, the market participant asks the datahub operator to update the customer 
identifier. The request is made outside the data hub. 
The Datahub operator updates the customer's identifier. 
Parties and roles 
Datahub, Seller (Seller), Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The Datahub operator has received the necessary information from the person requesting the change 
from the market participant. 
Information to be reported 
The party's own ID and the customer's ID. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have a sales contract with the customer, which is valid either 
at or after the requested update, or that has expired for no more than 6 weeks 
earlier. 
If the process is started from a request to update customer information from the distribution system operator, 
the distribution network operator must have a valid network contract with the customer 
either at the time of the requested update or after. 
Code 
The updated customer can be found in datahub and is a consumer by customer type. 
Only the customer's identifier type is updated from the party's own identifier 
(AA04) to personal identification number (AA03). 
If the customer whose identifier is the party's own ID (AA04) is encrypted and the customer, 
who has a personal ID, does not, the process is interrupted. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The connection is made by the customer whose identifier is the party's own identifier, 
since day one. 
Processing 
All contracts belonging to a customer with a party's own ID will be transferred/copied 
for a customer with a personal identification number. 
A customer with a party's own ID will be made inactive after merging. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
Customer information provided by the seller and the date from which the change is made. Old information 
are stored in datahub. 
Processed data 
Transferred contracts. 
Data return/forwarding 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

Data recovery 
Notification of successful or failed client connection datahub-
to the operator. 
Transmission of information 
The notice is sent to all parties who have a sales or online contract with the combined 
with the customer. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The merging of customers is done for the wrong customers. 
Cancellation terms 
The process cannot be undone.

4.6 
DH-121 Creation of a place of use 
TABLE 777 DESCRIPTION OF USE PLACE CREATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator creates a new access point in the data hub 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution network operator creates a new access point and enters the data required by the data hub 
to its own information systemInformation to be reported 
Place of use information (mandatory information depends on the state of the place of use); place of use 
address and measurement area to which the place of use belongs 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The ID of the place of use must not already exist in the data hub. 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. 
You cannot create a place of use in the state "Disabled" or "Removed from the system". 
The place of use may not be notified of information about a parallel place of use. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The new place of use must be notified immediately after the necessary information has been saved 
to the distribution system operator's own system. 
Effective date 3 years retroactively at the earliest, no later than the current day at 
00:00. 
Processing 
Datahub calculates the electric power of the place of use based on the fuse size, if there is no separate electric power 
announced. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database 
Processed data 
Electrical power, if not separately stated in the message. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected usage location creation. Information in the rejection message 
the reason for rejection. 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The address of the place of use is given incorrectly or an incorrect place of use is created (e.g. 
the place of use does not exist) → The contract is made for the wrong place of use.

4.7 
DH-122 Update of location information 
TABLE 888 DESCRIPTION OF THE UPDATE OF USAGE LOCATION INFORMATION BY THE DISTRIBUTION NETWORK OPERATOR 
THROUGH THE AGENCY OF 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator announces the update of the usage location information, the annual usage estimate 
about an update or responds to a request to update the location information. An update can 
change the basic information of the place of use and the status of the place of use. In response 
valid ones can also be indicated in the request for updating the location of use data 
location information, which means that the update request has been rejected. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution system operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator makes changes to the place of use, updates the information to its own 
system and sends a notification about this to datahub, or the distribution network operator is 
received a request to update usage location data from datahub. 
Information to be reported 
The date from which the changes take effect; location of use information, voluntary 
explanation of the update, reason code for the update if it is an update of the annual usage estimate. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use must fall within the measurement area of ​​the reporting distribution system operator 
Code 
The place of use must be found in datahub and the update must be valid 
on the effective date, and its status must not be "Disabled" or "Removed". 
from the system". 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. The place of use must fall within the stated measurement area. 
The status of the access point cannot be updated so that it changes to the status "Connected", "Disconnected" or 
"Removed from the system". These status updates youconnecting, disconnecting or 
with place of use removal events. 
If the place of use is being updated to the status "Disabled", the place of use is not allowed 
be valid in the system at the time the update takes effect or after 
contracts coming into force. 
If the place of use belongs to the energy community at the time the update takes effect or after 
after, the status of the place of use cannot be changed to "Disabled" until 
the place of use has been removed from the energy community.  
If the place of use has a parallel place of use at the time the update takes effect or 
after that, the status of the place of use cannot be changed to "Disabled". No inspection 
to be done if the parallel access point is already in the state "disabled" or "deleted 
of the system".  
You may not update data from the parallel with the update event of the usage location data 
from the place of use and not from the energy community. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

Time limits 
The information update must be reported immediately when the distribution system operator makes a change 
to your own system. The effective time of the update is the current day or at most 10 
years in the past. 
When the distribution network operator responds to the request to update the usage location information, the update will come 
send within 30 days of receiving the update request. The update will be taken 
I will reply later, but notifications sent repeatedly late will be received 
to intervene. 
Processing 
Datahub calculates the electric power of the place of use based on the fuse size, if the electric power is not specified separately. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
Electrical power, if not separately stated in the message. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected update of location information 
Transmission of information 
If the update contains changes to valid information, the information contained in the update 
other parties related to the place of use will be notified, taking into account the rights of the parties 
at the time of entry into force of the update indicated in the information. In response, the seller or 
The update request for the 3rd party's location information is also forwarded to an update that does not 
inside changes.  
If the update of the location of use is notified retroactively for more than 6 weeks, the seller 
after the end of the contract, it will not be forwarded to the seller even for an update 
the effective date would be during the validity period of the seller's contract. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Information is reported incorrectly → Sellers and 3rd parties may enter into incorrect contracts 
with the customer or incorrect measures, for example in the balance sheet or 
in the control of loads. 
Cancellation terms 
The information will be corrected with a new update.

4.8 
DH-123 Removal of place of use 
TABLE 999 DESCRIPTION OF DELETE OF INCORRECT USE PLACE 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution network operator informs the data hub of the deletion of the access point  
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator detects an erroneously created or otherwise unnecessary 
location of use and deletes the location of use from its own system. 
Information to be reported 
ID of the place of use, ID of the measurement area 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator 
Code 
The place of use can be found in the data hub and is not in the state "Disabled" or "Removed 
from the system". 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. The place of use must fall within the stated measurement area. 
There is no contract information associated with the place of use (including expired and cancelled 
contracts). 
The place of use must not be part of the energy community at the time the write-off takes effect or after 
after. 
The place of use must not have a parallel place of use at the time the removal takes effect or 
then. The check is not performed if the parallel usage location is already in the space 
"disabled" or "removed from the system". 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
-  
Time limits 
The notification must be made as soon as the distribution system operator removes the access point from its own 
from their system. 
The time of creation of the place of use should be stated as the effective date. 
Processing 
The status of the place of use is updated to "removed from the system". 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
The place of use of the notification is deleted from the system 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected usage location deletion 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023

4.9 
DH-124 Request for update of location information 
TABLE 101010 DESCRIPTION OF USER LOCATION DATA UPDATE BY SELLER OR THIRD PARTY 
THROUGH THE AGENCY OF 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or a 3rd party forwards the changes to the location of use information notified by the customer 
to the distribution system operator. The distribution system operator decides whether this changes the data to its own 
to their system and triggers the actual data update event vendor 
based on the announcement. The purpose of this event is to improve certainup-to-date information on the location of use.  
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / 3rd party (Energy service provider), Datahub, Distribution network operator 
(Network service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer informs the seller or a third party of a change in the location information, which 
transmits information about changes to the distribution system operator via the data hub 
Information to be reported 
The date from which the changes take effect; location ID and measurement area 
logo. In addition, from the following information, those to which a change is desired (see partial updates 
principle in chapter 2.15): address of the place of use; tax category, user group; 
annual usage estimate; steerable load; production equipment; storage device; free text/comment: 
the customer's report/explanation for the data change. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have a valid contract at the time of the requested change in datahub 
at the place of use. The 3rd party must have authorization for the data of the place of use. 
Code 
The place of use must be found in the data hub and its status must not be "Disabled" or 
"Removed from the system". 
The place of use must fall within the stated measurement area. 
It is not possible to ask the user to update the status to "Connected", "Disconnected" or "Removed 
from the system". Connection and disconnection requests are made with their own events. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
As soon as the seller or a third party becomes aware of the changes. An update request 
the effective date is a maximum of 10 years in the past and a maximum of 90 days 
in the future. 
Processing 
Datahub checks whether the information in the update request is the same as the information valid at the requested entry into force 
location information. If they are, a negative acknowledgment is returned and the request is not forwarded. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected transmission of location data

The annual usage estimate is reported incorrectly → there is a large deviation in the balance sheet calculation

4.10 
DH-125 Measurement time step update 
TABLE 111111 UPDATE OF THE USE LOCATION MEASUREMENT TIME STEP 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator updates the time step of the measurement of the point of use. In existence 
notification of the information is rejected. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution system operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution network operator updates the measurement time step of the point of use to its own 
to its information system and sends the information to datahub. 
Information to be reported 
The moment of the change with an hour precision, the time step of the measurement of the place of use 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use must fall within the measurement area of ​​the reporting distribution system operator. 
Code 
The place of use must be found in datahub and the update must be valid 
on the effective date, and its status must not be "Disabled" or "Removed". 
from the system". 
The measurement point must not have had measurement data reported in a previous time step 
for the period after the effective date of the update. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The information update must be reported immediately when the distribution system operator does 
change to own system. The effective time of the update is at most 1 
a month in the future or up to 11 days in the past. 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of success or failure for the time step of the measurement of the place of use 
about the update. 
Transmission of information 
The information contained in the update will be notified to other parties related to the place of use 
taking into account the rights of the parties to the information in the announced update 
at the time of entry into force. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The measurement data has been reported with a different time step for the time interval to which the change applies. JVH 
can ask the Datahub operator to delete the measurement data. from time interval 
in exceptional cases.

DH-126 Declaration of parallel use location information 
TABLE 121212 PARALLEL USE LOCATION INFORMATION NOTICE 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator announces the update of the parallel usage location information. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution system operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution network operator creates a connection for consumption and related to the same physical object 
between small production places of use and informs the places of use of the information 
parallelism.   
Information to be reported 
The date from which the changes take effect; user location codes; measurement range 
logo 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use must fall within the measurement area of ​​the reporting distribution system operator. 
Code 
The places of use must be found in the datahub and the update must be valid 
on the effective date, and their status must not be "Disabled" or "Removed". 
from the system". 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. The places of use must belong to the declared same 
to the measurement area. 
The second type of the indicated place of use must be "Consumption" and the other "Production". 
The declared places of use cannot already have parallel places of use. 
The declared place of consumption cannot belong to an energy community with a surplus 
sharing method is "SMB". 
If both of the declared places of use belong to the energy community, it is for both 
belong to the same energy community.  
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The information update must be reported immediately when the distribution system operator makes a change 
to your own system. The effective date of the update is the notification date at the earliest 
the next day or up to 90 days into the future. 
Processing 
Datahub includes the places of use on the announced effective date in the netting calculation, if announced 
production device/devices with a total maximum power of no more than 100 have been declared at the production site 
kVA. If the production site has production device(s) for which no maximum power data has been declared, 
places of use are not included in the netting calculation.  
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
 
Data return/forwarding 
 
  
Datahub events
