Event description 
Definition 
The seller or a third party applies for a place of use on the basis of the address. Seller or 
The 3rd party needs the ID of the place of use in order to be able to search for more details 
location of use and customer information from datahub. The seller or a third party can also apply 
information about the place of use by entering the place of use ID in the search, if it is known. 
Parties and roles 
New seller (Seller) / Current seller (Seller) / 3rd party (Energiapalvelnprovider), 
Datahub 
Event initiation 
Starts when 
The seller or a 3rd party needs the customer's usage point ID or usage point 
basic information based on the usage point ID. 
Information to be reported 
Address of the usage point, part of the address or usage point ID. Optionally, 
the meter number, usage point type, 
parallel usage point ID or usage point subtype can also be used as search factors. 
Validation 
Rights to data 
- 
Rules 
- 
Interrupting 
events 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported data 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/transmission 
Data return 
Basic information of the usage point according to the class diagram below or rejection of the search. 
The search returns a limited number (max 50) of access points found based on the address. Deleted (state deleted from the system) access points are not included in the 
response. 
If there are more than 50 access points matching the search criteria or no access points matching the search criteria are found, the search is rejected.

4.14 
DH-132 Location of use and customer data search - current seller 
TABLE 151515 DESCRIPTION OF CURRENT SELLER'S LOCATION INFORMATION SEARCH 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller applies for the place of use of his current, future or former contract, 
customer and contract information. 
Parties and roles 
Current or former vendor (Vendor), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller wants to check the data related to a specific place of use from the data hub. 
Information to be reported 
The usage location number and time of day for which the information is desired 
seek. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have had a valid contract for the place of use applied for 
at the time so that the seller can get full information. If the seller has a data hub 
announced sales contract starting in the future at the place of use, this can already be applied for 
information by transaction using the future date when the contract will be 
to be valid. 
If the seller's contract at the place of use has ended less than 6 weeks ago and asked 
the moment of time is also in the period of 6 weeks after the end of the sales contract, 
only the customer information and the basic information of the place of use will be returned to the seller if requested 
at the moment. 
Code 
The place of use must be found based on the place of use ID given in the data hub. 
The point of use is not in the state "Removed from the system". 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Complete information on the place of use, information on the sales contract, to the sales contract 
attached customer information, online contract information (only if sales contract 
the corresponding online contract has been confirmed) as well as information about the online product from the person asked 
at the moment.  
Alternatively, the rejection of the search is returned. An error message is returned, if any 
the place of use cannot be found with the search criteria. 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations

4.15 
DH-133 Place of use and customer information search - new seller 
TABLE 161616 DESCRIPTION OF NEW SELLER LOCATION INFORMATION SEARCH 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or a 3rd party, authorized by the customer, applies for a contract from datahub 
to make the information they need about the place of use, the customer and the customer 
about the contractual situation at the place of use. 
Parties and roles 
Potential seller (Seller) / 3rd party (Energy service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller starts making a new contract with the customer or a 3rd party tenders 
sales contract on behalf of the customer. 
Information to be reported 
Place of use place of use number; customer identifier. If the contract is made for several people 
to the customer, the information of all customers is reported. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The new seller or 3rd party must have authorization from at least one person in the survey 
from the notified customer to the place of use in question. 3rd party authorization will be required 
be of the type "Contract bidding as a service". Without the customer's authorization 
to the point of use, the transaction is rejected. 
If at least one notified customer who has authorized the party has 
valid contract at the place of use, full information is returned. 
In moving-in situations, no customer has a contractat the workplace, 
in which case limited data is returned (see class diagram below). 
Code 
The place of use must be found based on the place of use ID given in the data hub. 
The point of use is not in the state "Removed from the system". 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
1. From the customer information, the information of the customers entered in the search is returned 
and whose data the new seller or 3rd party has authorization for in datahub. 
2. The following information is returned from the location information: 
a. the customer does not have a contract for the place of use → Basic information of the place of use 
b. the customer has a contract for the place of use → Complete information about the place of use 
3. The following information about the contract status of the place of use is returned:

Definition

Information to be reported

Validation 
Rights to information

Code 
The place of use can be found in datahub. The place of use is not in the state “Deleted 
from the system". 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery

information about the seller of the place of use and the products for sale if the seller has given authorization 
to product information.

not found, the search is rejected.

DH-135 Place of use and customer information search - 3rd party 
TABLE 181818 DESCRIPTION OF LOCATION INFORMATION SEARCH BY A 3RD PARTY 
Event description 
Definition 
The 3rd party requests information about the place of use and the customer with authorization. 
Parties and roles 
3rd party (Energy service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The 3rd party needs information about the customer and the place of use in their customer service. 
Information to be reported 
ID of the place of use; customer identifier; the date from which the information is to be retrieved. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
All customers reported in the survey must have a valid sales or 
online contract at the place of use at the time indicated in the survey. 
The 3rd party must have authorization for the place of use from at least one person in the survey 
of the reported customers at the time indicated in the survey. 
Code 
The place of use can be found in datahub. The place of use is not in the state “Deleted 
from the system". 
An interruptionvt

- 
Processing 
-

Data recovery 
Information about the place of use and information about the customer of the place of use, as well as information about the online product. If 
more than one customer is attached to the contract, the customer information is only returned 
for those customers from whom the party has authorization. 
Alternatively, the rejection of the search is returned. If a customer matching the application criteria and 
no place of use is found, the search is rejected.

4.18 
DH-141 Creating an energy community 
TABLE 191919 DESCRIPTION CREATION OF THE ENERGY COMMUNITY 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution network operator creates a new energy community in the data hub. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub (MIA), seller (DDQ), 
3rd party (THP) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator creates a new energy community and enters the data required by the data hub 
to its own information system. 
Information to be reported 
The name and identifier of the energy community, the places of use belonging to the community, 
share percentage by place of use, place of use for surplus energy, surplus 
calculation method 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. 
The ID of the energy community must not already exist in the data hub.  
The start of the energy community's ID must be the GLN of the notifying distribution system operator
logo.  
The member-use sites that are reported to the energy community must not already be part of it 
to another energy community.  
The member-use locations reported to the energy community may not be in the community twice.  
If the energy community's surplus calculation method is SMA, not in any community 
in the declared member locations, the subtype of the location may be "Virtual". 
All usage locations belonging to the Energy Community belong to the same measurement area.  
The energy community has at least two member consumption locations.  
The energy community has at least one member-small production site.  
Only one place of use, which is not a subtype, should be reported to the energy community 
"Virtual", as Surplus usage location. 
If the small production site registered as a member of the Energy Association has 
parallel place of use, that parallel place of use cannot belong to another 
To the energy community.  
The member-use location reported to the energy community can be found in the data hub, and there is no 
in the status "Removed" or "Disabled" on the date of entry into force of the entity. 
If the method of calculation of the surplus of the Energy Company to be reported is SMB, will 
for the declared member-consumption use place to be parallel 
small production use site, which must also be reported by the same Energy Community 
become a member. (If necessary, the distribution system operator must be created with transaction DH-121 
a place of use with a subtype of "Virtual", before the creation of the energy community.)  
The shares of member workplaces belonging to the community are 100%. 
The share of an individual member location cannot be 100%. 
 
  
Datahub events 
 
7 November 2023 
 
 
 
 
 
  
 
156 (468) 
 
Fingrid Datahub Oy 
Street address

Fax

firstname.surname@fingrid.fi

030 395 5000 
030 395 5196 
www.fingrid.fi 
 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The energy community can be notified to the datahub no earlier than 7 days or at most 
90 days into the future. 
Processing 
The energy community and its member-use locations are included in the community accounts of the Energy Community 
from the effective date.  
The information of the energy community is stored in member-location information.  
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected energy community creation. 
Transmission of information 
The information contained in the update will be notified to others connected to member locations 
to the parties, taking into account the parties' rights to the information with the notified update 
at the time of entry into force.  
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Incorrect places of use are added to the community, so the results of the calculation are reported 
with incorrect location information.  
Cancellation terms 
The information is corrected either by updating Energy community data or Energy community data 
by deciding.

DH-142 Energy Community Update 
TABLE 202020 DESCRIPTION OF THE ENERGY COMMUNITY UPDATE 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator updates the information of the energy community. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, vendors, 3rd parties 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator updates the information of the energy community in its information system. 
Information to be reported 
Name and identifier of the energy community, usage locations belonging to the community, share percentage, 
surplus calculation method 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. 
The energy community must be valid on the update date indicated in the data hub.  
The member-use locations reported to the energy community may not be in the community twice.  
The method of calculating the surplus may not be changed with an update transaction.  
If the energy community's surplus calculation method is SMA, not in any community 
in the declared member locations, the subtype of the location may be "Virtual". 
All usage locations belonging to the Energy Community belong to the same measurement area.  
The energy community has at least two member consumption locations.  
The energy community has at least one member-small production site.  
Only one place of use, which is not a subtype, should be reported to the energy community 
"Virtual", as Surplus usage location. 
If the small production site registered as a member of the Energy Association has 
parallel place of use, that parallel place of use cannot belong to another 
To the energy community.  
The member-use location reported to the energy community can be found in the data hub, and there is no 
in the status "Removed" or "Disabled" on the date of entry into force of the entity. 
If the method of calculation of the surplus of the Energy Company to be reported is SMB, will 
for the declared member-consumption use place to be parallel 
small production use site, which must also be reported by the same Energy Community 
become a member. (If necessary, the distribution system operator must be created with transaction DH-121 
a place of use with a subtype of "Virtual" before the update of the energy community.)  
The shares of member workplaces belonging to the community are 100%. 
The share of an individual member location cannot be 100%. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The energy community change can be reported to datahub no earlier than 7 days or 
up to 90 days into the future. 
Processing

4.20 
DH-143 Termination of the Energy Community 
TABLE 212121 DESCRIPTION OF THE TERMINATION OF THE ENERGY COMMUNITY 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator decides the energy community. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, vendors, 3rd parties 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator determines the energy community in its information system. 
Information to be reported 
Energy community ID and end date 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The energy community must be valid on the end date indicated in the data hub.  
The energy community belongs to the reporting distribution system operator.  
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
Termination of the energy community can be reported to datahub no earlier than 7 days or 
up to 90 days into the future. 
Processing 
The energy community and the member-use locations belonging to it are removed from the community accounts of the energy community 
from the effective date of termination.  
The information of the energy community is deleted from the member-location information.  
Data storage 
Reported information 
All reported information is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected termination.  
Transmission of information 
The information contained in the decision will be communicated to others related to member locations 
to the parties, taking into account the parties' rights to the information with the notified update 
at the time of entry into force.  
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The community information is decided too early and the calculations are interrupted unnecessarily.  
Cancellation terms 
The data is corrected with the notification of the Energy Community Data by reporting a new one 
Energy community.

DH-211 Notification of measurement information 
TABLE 222222 DESCRIPTION OF NOTIFICATION OF MEASUREMENT INFORMATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The person responsible for measurement (distribution system operator) indicates the measurement point (location of use, 
border point, or production unit) measurement data to the data hub. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution system operator (responsible for metering data), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 
3.Party (Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The person responsible for the measurement data has collected and validated the measurement data and reports this 
to datahub. If the person responsible for the measurement data has not been allowed to collect the measured and 
validated data into your own system, the person responsible for the measurement data enters the data hub 
in these respects, informs that the measurement data in question is missing. 
Information to be reported 
Measurement point-specific measurement data (incl. measurement point ID), measurement data 
interval 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The measurement point belongs to the measurement area and measurement responsibility of the person responsible for the measurement. 
Code 
Measurement point-specific validation (see the document "Sähkön 
retail market business processes" chapter 3.3.2.2); the measurement point is found 
from datahub; the measurement point is not under construction; there is no specified time period 
in the future and not more than 6 years in the past; single 
a notification event can contain a maximum of 10,000 measurement time series and each 
measurement time series up to 10,000 time series values.  
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
Section 3.3.2.3 of the document "Business processes of the electricity retail market". 
and 3.3.2.4 time limits must be observed, but corrections are allowed for the entire measurement data 
for the storage period. 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
The measurement data of the measurement points and the time interval from which the measurement data are. 
Processed data 
Datahub updates the reactive power kits available field of the usage location to "yes", 
if reactive power data is reported to the point of use and the value of the above field is in the data hub 
"No". 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Positive or negative acknowledgment per transaction. 
Transmission of information 
Measurement data sent to Datahub and accepted are forwarded to sellers and third parties, 
who have the right to measurement data. Two points in time are announced in the forwarding message, 
the time when the measurement data has been received in the data hub and the time when the data

The following transaction validations are performed on the transaction data. Datahub discards the message data 
by measurement time series. So the message is not completely rejected if there is even one mistake in it, but only 
measurement time series containing errors are rejected. 
# 
Transaction validation 
1 
The measuring point can be found in the system. 
2 
The party (distribution system operator or 3rd party) has the right to supply measurement data 
to the measurement area. 
3 
The resolution of the measurement data is the same as the time step indicated for the measurement point. 
4 
The period to be declared is neither in the future nor more than 6 years in the past 
5 
The time series contains a value (or missing value information) for each position in the reporting interval. 
6 
The measurement point is not under construction.

DH-221, DH-222, DH-223 Measurement data searches 
TABLE 232323 DESCRIPTION OF MEASUREMENT INFORMATION SEARCH 
Event description 
Definition 
Seller/Distribution system operator/3.Party retrieves measurement data from the data hub, to which 
he is entitled. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / Distribution System Operator (Responsible for Metering Data) / 3rd Party 
(Energy service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The party has tArve for a separate measurement data search in addition to the datahub 
forwards all new and 
changed measurement data.  
Information to be reported 
If desired, the search can be limited by measurement area, place of use, limit point or 
with the ID of the production unit and the type of place of use; interval; active power and 
the unit of reactive power and the time step in which the data is retrieved. Datahub does not return valid 
or reactive power data, if the corresponding (reactive power or reactive power) unit is not given 
in search. In the application, you must provide at least either the active or reactive power unit. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
Chapter 2.2 of the document "Business processes of the retail electricity market". 
in accordance with. 
Code 
- 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
- 
Processing 
Converting the unit and/or time step from the data hub's internal unit to the unit requested by the seller and 
to the time step. If the time step is not specified in the search, the time series is returned with the time step, as 
it is stored in datahub. 
The measurement data search is carried out asynchronously due to large data masses. Datahub prioritizes 
Synchronous calls precede the search for measurement data, and the search for measurement data is processed in the so-called in the background. 
The duration of processing depends on the amount of data retrieved. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding

Data recovery 
Searched measurement data of measurement points or rejection of the search. Search returns 
measurement data to the extent that the party is entitled to them. Active and/or reactive powers

measurement data is retrieved as sum data and the output values ​​have one or more (no

missing" 
Search results are returned for a maximum of 10,000 measurement time series and each 
measurement time series as words containing a maximum of 10,000 time series values. 
There may be one or more messages to be returned, depending on the amount of information requested.

DH-212-1 – DH-212-5 Reminder of measurement data notification 
TABLE 242424 DESCRIPTION OF MEASUREMENT INFORMATION NOTIFICATION REMINDER 
Event description 
Definition 
Datahub reports incorrect or undeclared measurement data 
to the person responsible for the measurement data (distribution system operator or distribution system operator 
commissioned by a 3rd party) 
Parties and roles 
Datahub, Distribution System Operator (Responsible for Metering Data) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
In Datahub's daily validation, deficiencies are detected by the distribution system operator 
in measurement data 
Information to be reported 
Datahub informs them of the interval and measurement point ID for each time series 
from measurement points whose measurement data are incorrect or incomplete. Boundary points 
direction is also announced. 
The reason for the reminder is identified by the process ID: 
• 
DH-212-1: No time series reported 
• 
DH-212-2 Missing status: Missing time series 
• 
DH-212-3: Incomplete status: Uncertain time series 
• 
DH-212-4: Non-zero value: cutoff 
• 
DH-212-5: Non-zero value: wrong direction (limit point) 
Validation 
Rights to information 
Measurement is the responsibility of the distribution system operator 
Code 
Section 3.3.2.4 of the document "Electricity retail market business processes".

proceedings 
-

6.1 
DH-311 Notice of new contract  
TABLE 292929 DESCRIPTION OF NOTIFICATION OF A NEW AGREEMENT TO THE PLACE OF USE 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller announces a new sales contract concluded by the customer 
with to the customer's place of use. If necessary, a new one is created in the data hub 
network contract information and the Distribution System Operator receives information about the new one 
of the contract. 
Parties and roles 
New seller / Current seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution network operator 
(Network service provider), Current seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer concludes a new contract with the seller for the customer's current or 
to a new place of use. 
Information to be reported 
Location ID, customer information and contract information, including contract-specific information 
billing addresses and contact information. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
If the customer has contracts stored in the data hub for the place of use, 
the notification will not be accepted, i.e. a new contract cannot be concluded, if: 
• 
The place of use has a fixed-term valid sales contract, and 
the contract has the same customer as the new contract 
in the announcement (the start date must be later than 
the expiry date of the previous contract, if 
such exists). However, if the contract's customers are 
consumers and the term period has continued for more than 2 years, the contract 
the term does not prevent a new contract. 
• 
There is an exception in the valid contract of the place of use 
termination clause, and there is even one customer in the contract that is the same as the new one 
in the notice of the contract, and a different termination condition 
the dates do not allow a new contract to be concluded for the place of use. 
• 
The above rules are deviated from if the current seller needs to do so 
changes to the customers of the contract to the place of use, however, in such a way that 
the new contract has at least one customer who is the same as 
in the valid contract of the place of use. 
Before the new sales contract previously notified to the place of use 
entry into force, a new sales contract can be announced "in between", but in this case 
the end date of the contract must be stated and it cannot be later 
than the start date of the previously announced contract (in the document "Sähkön 
retail market business processes" in chapter 3.2.2.4 example 3). 
Only the seller responsible for delivery assigned to the measurement area of ​​the place of use can 
announces the electricity supply contract. 
The place of use can be found in datahub and is valid on the start date of the contract. 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area and is not in the state disabled or 
removed from the system on the contract start date. If the place of use already exists

disabled, the new (retroactive) contract must expire 
on or before the date of decommissioning. 
If both business customers and consumer customers are notified in the contract, 
consumer rules apply to the contract. 
The consumer customer must be at least 18 years old. 
The seller's balance sheet manager has announced the necessary seller and balance sheet manager

valid on the date of commencement of the sales contract. 
If the place of use has already been notified of the termination of the sales contract with a reason

on or before the removal date. 
If the place of use has already been notified as corresponding to the new sales contract 
termination of the online contract, the new contract must expire accordingly 
on or before the end date of the online contract.  
If the notice of the new sales contract also states the contract 
end date, the end date can be a maximum of 90 days ahead 
from the moment of notification.  
Interrupting 
proceedings 
For the same place of use for the same contract start date earlier 
notified sales contract. Two new contracts cannot be announced as startingfor the same day, but those reported later will be rejected. As an exception 
move-in (all customers change), which also cancels earlier 
of the sales contract announced for the same starting date for the place of use, which 
the reason for the start is a change of vendor/contract (if previously announced 
the agreement is a move-in, it prevents the notification of another move-in to the same one 
for the start date). 
Time limits 
If the reason for starting the contract is moving in or changing the contract, a new one 
the sales contract can be announced for the current day at the earliest. If that's the case 
there is a change of seller, the new sales contract can be announced on the 14th at the earliest 
to start after one day, unless there is already a previous sales contract 
ended, in which case the new sales contract can start no earlier than the previous one 
ending. The notification can be sent no earlier than 90 days before 
the start date of the sales contract to be notified. 
In error correction situations, it is possible to announce a new sales contract 
to start retroactively. It is possible to declare retroactive move-in 
a maximum of 3.5 years retroactively. A retroactive change of seller is possible 
report no more than 10 years back. No retroactive change of contract 
allow in datahub. 
Processing 
Creating a customer 
If the customer of the contract to be notified is not found in datahub, it will be created 
to datahub. 
The start of the contract 
reason 
The system determines the reason for the start of the sales contract in the document "Sähkön 
retail market business processes" according to table 8 of chapter 3.2.2. 
Current contract 
deciding 
Datahub determines the validity of the current vendor of the usage location 
for the day before the start date of the new contract of the sales contract. 
A new contract is recorded as the reason for the termination of the current contract 
based on the starting reason. 
• 
"Moving out", if the reason for starting the new contract is "Moving in"

Contracts 
cancellation 
Changing customers at the point of use automatically cancels everything 
start on the same or a later date than the current one of the place of use 
the customer's new sales contracts (in the document "Sähkön 
retail market business processes" in chapter 3.2.2.4 example 4). 
Confirmed or 
Unconfirmed network contracts will be cancelled. 
Network contract 
creation 
If a new network contract is needed, datahub creates a new network contract 
information (start date same as sales contract, network contract 
to "unconfirmed"). When creating a new online contract 
datahub terminates the valid network contract for the previous day. 
Rules for reasoning: 
• 
The responsibility of the contracts does not change (the new contract is the same or 
to be answered by the same customers as valid at the time of notification 
existing), in which case it is a pure change of seller or a new contract 
with the current seller → no new online contract is needed. 
• 
The responsibility of contracts changes (one or more contracting parties 
changes, is added or removed) → a new network contract is needed in order to 
the same customers are responsible for the contracts. 
• 
At the time of announcement, the online contract is already a new contract 
in the name of the customer, but the customer of the sales contract changes → new 
no online contract required. 
• 
The sales contract valid at the time of notification is 
the electricity supply contract and the new sales contract are not, or vice versa 
(if there is no sales contract in force at the time of notification, but 
a valid online contract is found, the same check is made for a new one 
sales contract and valid online contract 
Between the 'Electricity supply agreement' field) → a new one is needed 
online contract. 
• 
The customers of the new sales contract to be announced are the same as 
customers with a valid network contract, but 
the online contract has the expiry date of the new sales contract 
during the duration → a new network contract is required. Datahub decides 
the previous network agreement and sends a new network agreement 
to be confirmed. 
• 
The customers of the new sales contract to be announced are the same as 
customers of a valid network contract, but a network contract 
pending cancellation of the sales contract announced by the seller 
based on cancellation → a new online contract is required.  
Authorizations 
deciding 
If the place of use has authorizations that are valid for the new contract 
at the commencement or enter into force after the commencement of the new contract, they 
be terminated at the time the contract starts or canceled, if authorized 
the customer is also not a customer in the new sales contract. Authorizations 
is canceled if the authorization is not yet valid by setting the authorization 
end date to be the same asstart date. 
If the customer is notified confidentially with a new contract, all of that 
the customer's authorizations at any place of use, the contract is concluded

Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected notification. If the notification is successful, 
the reason for the new contract registered in datahub is returned (moving in, 
change of seller, change of contract). 
The rejection of the contract contains information about the reason for the rejection. Current contract 
the expiration date is returned if it is less than 90 
one day from the moment of notification. If the current contract has 
deviating termination condition, the first possible contract is returned 
start date. 
Transmission of information 
The current seller of the possible place of use will be informed of the current one 
of the termination of the sales contract. 
The distribution system operator of the place of use is notified of the new network contract, 
if an online contract is created in the process. Otherwise 
the distribution system operator receives information about the new sales contract at the point of use. 
If the announcement of a new sales contract updates an existing one in the datahub 
the customer's information, the updated information will be forwarded to all those entitled to the information 
to the parties. 
Notification to the customer's potential seller of the parallel usage location 
emigration. 
Upon moving in, notification of the cancellation of the sales contract 
for a seller who has a new contract starting in the future other than

Notification of the termination of the current sales contract is forwarded to third parties,

Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The sales contract is notified to the wrong place of use → Wrong place of use 
the customer's current contract is terminated without cause 
Incorrect customer information is forwarded to all parties who are entitled 
to customer information.  
Maintaining the correctness of the data is the responsibility of the personal data registrar 
responsible. Forwarding incorrect information is a violation of data protection.  
The customer's mailing address is reported incorrectly → Possible mails (incl. invoices) 
go to the wrong address, especially if it is not known in the contract 
separate billing address. The result may be incorrect collection actions or 
data breach. 
The customer's contact information is reported incorrectly or incomplete → No to the customer 
get in touch, because the existing contact information will be deleted. 
The customer's name information is reported incorrectly → Possible mails (incl. invoices) are not 
get there or they go to the wrong recipient. 
Cancellation terms 
Before the start date of the contract. Cancellation of a valid contract 
managing the business processes of the document "Electricity retail market" 
according to section 3.2.5.1.

start date'. 
"Date of start date" must be the same as "Agreement 
start date'. 
[3] 
If it is an electricity supply contract, the invoicing method should be "Seller invoices 
both". 
If the invoicing method is something other than separate invoicing, the distribution network operator of the point of use must 
allow joint billing. 
[4] 
An unusual termination condition can only be stated in the business customer's sales contract. 
[5] 
If the contract has a different termination clause, either must be specified for the contract 
notice period in days or notice period. The notice period defines the time period when 
the contract can be terminated. If a notice period is used, the seller must take care of the period 
updating to the contract. 
Information may not be reported to a contract that does not have a different termination clause. 
[6] 
The consumer's e-invoice address is not imported into the data hub. However, it can be marked as a billing channel 
E-invoice or Direct Payment. In this case, the billing address is mandatory. 
[7] 
If the customer of the contract is a company, at least one must be indicated in the contract 
contact. Contact persons are persons that the parties need 
in customer service situations and may differ between sales and online contracts.  
Contact persons cannot be of the same contact person type. 
Each contact person must be informed of at least one of the name details. 
The parties may have their own contact information, but only those whose 
mediation between the parties is necessary. 
[8] 
In addition to the postal code, the address information must include either the street name and house number, or 
P.O. box. 
The stair code is mandatory if the apartment is declared. 
[9] 
To be declared if the invoicing channel is an online invoice. 
[10]

(email address to be reported).  
[11]

(used as identifying information in a situation where the personal identification number is not known/y identification number is not available 
be). 
[12] 
If the type of customer is a consumer, the type of customer identifier must be personal identification number or 
party's own ID. If the customer type is company, the customer identifier type should be 
y ID or the party's own ID. 
[13] 
The customer type of a customer already in the system cannot be changed. 
If the contract specifies both a business customer and a consumer customer, it applies 
consumer-customer rules for the contract. 
[14] 
Bankruptcy estate allowed only for business customers.

The following transaction validations are performed on the transaction data.  
# 
Transaction validation 
1 
In the addresses, the post office is correct based on the postal code. The check is only done in Finland 
to the address located. 
2 
If a personal identification number is reported, it must comply with the format requirements for a personal identification number. 
3 
The effective date is in accordance with the business process specifications. 
4 
The end date of the agreement must be after the effective date. Likewise 
the end time of the fixed term must be after the starting time of the fixed term and not later 
the end time of the notice period must be after the start time of the notice period. 
5 
The announced contract start time and possible contract end time is midnight. Also 
unusually detachedthe nomisehdon and the start and end times of the duration of the agreement 
must be midnight. 
6 
If a product has been declared for the contract, the product must be found in the datahub and must be valid for the contract 
at the beginning and belong to the party that announced the contract. 
 
If the new sales contract enters into force retroactively (the effective date is earlier than 
current day) the contract is accepted, but the contract is not activated in the data hub. Agreement 
is only activated when the new seller has confirmed the contract and the old seller has accepted 
contract. Confirmation and acceptance of the contract is done manually using the online service 
through.

6.1.4 
DH-311-4 Notice of moving out of a parallel place of usen to the seller 
Datahub notifies the seller of the parallel access point of the termination of the agreement. The parallel access point agreement is not terminated automatically, but the seller of the parallel access point can 
if he wishes to terminate his agreement himself after receiving information about the move out. The notification uses the 
same information content as in the normal termination of the sales agreement (DH-331). The message 
presents the information about the parallel access point agreement.

6.1.5 
DH-311-5 Notification of cancellation of sales contract to incoming seller 
In connection with the move-in of a new customer, Datahub will notify the seller of the cancellation of the sales contract who has a sales contract that is starting in the future that is not the contract of the moving-in customer. The notification is made in the sales contract cancellation message with the reason "Customer's 
Cancellation".

Datahub ito notify the cancellation of the online contract when a new customer moves in 
to the distribution system operator, if the future network contract is canceled because the corresponding future one 
the sales contract (see DH-311-5) is cancelled. The notification is made with a notice of cancellation of the online contract 
with the reason "Customer cancellation".

DH-311-10 Notification of the termination of the sales contract to the authorized person 
to a 3rd party 
When the sales contract ends at the point of use due to the announcement of a new sales contract, datahub 
conveys the information about the termination of the contract to 3rd parties who are authorized to terminate the contract 
from the customer at the end of the contract. The content of the announcement corresponds to announcement DH-331-4.

6.2 
DH-312 Confirmation of network contract 
TABLE 303030 DESCRIPTION OF ONLINE AGREEMENT CONFIRMATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution network operator confirms or informs the new network contract in the data hub 
does not confirm the online agreement. The details of the online contract are forwarded to the seller or 
information about not confirming the online contract. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Current seller (Seller)  
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator has received information about the new data hub 
of the online contract, in which case he creates a new contract with this information 
to the system and confirms this to the datahub, or rejects the one created by the datahub 
network agreement. 
Information to be reported 
Confirmed information, location ID, network contract information included 
contract-specific billing addresses and contact information, (of the seller's transaction 
reference) 
If the online agreement is not confirmed: Explanation 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The access point can be found in the data hub and is not in the disabled or deleted state 
of the system. 
The measurement area must exist in the system and belong to the reporting party 
to the distribution system operator. The place of use must fall within the stated measurement area. 
The start time of the online contract must correspond to a of the sales contractstart time. 
The network contract cannot be confirmed if there is already a fully or partially overlapping network contract at the point of use. 
Interrupting 
events 
The point of use sales contract has been cancelled 
Time limits 
The distribution system operator must confirm the network contract as quickly as possible, 
at least two business days after receiving the information on the new network contract. Confirmation will be accepted later, but repeated 
late confirmations will be ignored. 
Processing 
Termination of the current contract 
Datahub terminates the valid network contract on the day before the start date of the new contract. 
Reason for starting the contract 
The same reason is recorded as the reason for starting the 
sales contract. 
Data storage 
Reported data 
All reported data is stored in the database. 
Processed data 
Expiration date of current network agreement 
New network agreement information (status=”confirmed”)

DH-321 Sales contract data update  
TABLE 313131 DESCRIPTION OF UPDATE OF SALES CONTRACT DATA 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller updates the contract information in datahub. 
The parties and 
roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller makes changes to the existing sales contract. 
Notifiable 
information 
ID of the place of use, Contract information, effective date of the change. 
The event 
processing 
worth noting 
The update of contract information should not automatically cause another event, such as 
for example, updating the customer's postal address (DH-111), unless the information has changed 
also for that. 
Data of the sales contract entered into by the party in its own system 
you should not send an update message to the datahub about updates if the update does not change anything 
contract information maintained in datahub 
Validation 
Rights 
to information 
The sales contract is the contract of the notifying seller 
Code 
The place of use can be found in the data hub, the place of use belongs to the measurement area and is not in the space 
disabled or removed from the system. 
The agreement must be found in datahub and be valid at the time the update takes effect. 
The start and end times of the contract may not be indicated with this notice, but they 
must be corrected by first sending a cancellation and then a new contract notice. 
The electricity supply contract cannot be upgraded to a regular contract or vice versa. 
A standard contract can be upgraded to a fixed-term contract and a fixed-term contract to a regular contract. 
It is also possible to update the contract with a new consecutive term period 
after the previous deadline period. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
There are both contracts valid at the time of notification and those starting in the future 
possible to update. It is possible to update a contract that has already ended at the time of notification 
only if less than 6 weeks have passed since the end of the contract. 
The effective date of the update can be a maximum of 10 years in the past, if applicable 
is from the electricity supply contract and no more than 3 years in the past, if applicable 
of the usual contract. The effective time of the update can be a maximum of 90 days 
in the future. 
Processing 
- 
Data storage

processing

changed in that regard as well. 
Updates to the data of the online agreement made by the party in its own system 
you should not send an update message to the datahub if the update does not change the datahub 
contract information to be maintained.

Rights 
to information

Code

of the system.

notify with a new contract notice.

proceedings

DH-323 Notification of non-vendor location 
TABLE 333333 DESCRIPTION OF NOTIFICATION OF UNSOLD LOCATION 
Event description 
Definition 
Datahub informs the distribution system operator of a non-vendor access point in order to 
the distribution system operator can terminate its own contract and terminate it if it wishes 
electricity at the place of use. The distribution system operator receives a one-off notification (DH-323-
1) from the point of use, when the system detects that the point of use is about to run out 
seller after 2 weeks or earlier. When the actual place of use is without 
seller, notification (DH-323-2) is sent to the distribution system operator every day.  
Parties and roles 
Datahub, Distribution network operator (Network service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
Whenever the datahub's internal processing finds a usage location that doesn't have one 
a valid sales contract (technically speaking, balance sheet information), but the place of use 
status is connected. Datahub's internal processing is performed once a day 
by 12 o'clock. 
Information to be reported 
ID of the place of use, ID of the measurement area, time from which the place of use 
is without a seller and the point of use is in the state "connected", the period without a seller 
end date if known. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator

proceedings

6.6 
DH-331 Notice of termination of the sales contract 
TABLE 343434 DESCRIPTION OF THE NOTICE OF TERMINATION OF THE SALES AGREEMENT 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller informs datahub of the end of the sales contract. Also datahub 
if necessary, the operator can use the event to conclude the sales contract. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution Network Operator (Network Service Provider), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider). 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller terminates the sales contract when the customer informs of moving out, if the customer wants 
terminates its sales contract with the Seller, the Seller has dismissed the customer 
of the agreement, the Seller terminates the agreement due to the end of its operation or the Seller 
receives the distribution system operator's move-out notification from the data hub. 
Information to be reported 
End date of the contract, possible final billing address and the contract 
the reason for the termination (moving out, termination of the contract, termination of the contract, 
removal of the meter, termination of the seller's activities) 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The contract belongs to the notifying seller. 
Code 
The place of use can be found in the data hub, the place of use belongs to the measurement area and is not in the space 
“disabled” or “removed from the system”. 
The contract to be concluded can be found in datahub, is related to the indicated place of use and is 
valid at the stated end time. 
The reason for the termination of the contract "Meter removal" is allowed only in response to DH-
333 for terminating a network contract, the reason for which is the removal of the meter. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
Reason "Moving out" or "Dismantling": Current day - 90 days ahead 
Reason "Termination" or "End of activity of the seller": 14 - 90 days 
ahead 
Reason "Remove meter": Back one month - current day. 
If the event is a response to the termination of the DH-333 network contract, 
the end date of the sales contract cannot be later than the online contract 
term. In case of meter removal, moving out and dismantling 
the end date must correspond to the end date of the online contract. Emigration and 
in case of dissolution, termination of the sales contract is then allowed 
nordifferent from the target time limits also for the past day.   
Processing 
Future contracts 
cancellation 
Moving out of a customer automatically cancels all the moving out customers 
in the future, the contracts will start at the place of use when the customers who are moving out are 
exactly the same as the customers of the future contract. 
If the reason for the termination of the contract is "Termination" or "Seller's actions". 
end" and the place of use has already been notified of a new one starting after the end date 
contract with the reason "Contract change" for at least one of the same customers as 
with the expiring contract, the future exchange of the contract will be canceled automatically.

Authorizations 
deciding 
Outmigration automatically decides the place of use for customers who are moving out 
applicable authorizations at the end of the contract. 
Outmigration automatically cancels customers moving out in the future 
authorizations begin at the end of the contract. 
Open switching 
or 
disconnection requests 
cancellation 
If there are openings at the place of use (there is no actual connection or disconnection yet 
announced) connection or disconnection requests with the requested connection or disconnection date 
is on or after the end date of the contract, these requests will be cancelled. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
End date of the sales contract, possible final billing address and 
reason for termination. The final billing address is saved as a new contract 
as the billing address, which comes into effect on the day the contract ends. 
Processed data 
In retroactive decisions, balance sheet information of the place of use. 
Possible changes to authorizations. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Information about a successful transaction or notification rejection. 
Transmission of information 
If, at the time of termination of the contract, the place of use has an equivalent to the sales contract 
network contract valid or unconfirmed, the distribution system operator is notified 
of the termination of the sales contract, possible final billing address and the termination 
reason. All event information is forwarded to the distribution system operator. 
If it is a move out, a possible parallel place of use will be forwarded 
notification to the seller of the termination of the contract in the event of moving out. Only 
the reason for the termination of the contract (emigration), the date of termination, the location ID and 
the ID of the original message is transmitted from the original message. Moving out 
the ID of the stated seller is not forwarded. 
The termination of the sales contract will be notified to third parties who have the customer 
authorization for the data of the respective location of use. The notification contains the same information that 
forwarded to the seller of the parallel usage location. 
Based on moving out, the cancellation of the sales contract is also announced 
for a seller of a place of use who has a sales contract starting in the future, which is not 
moving in. 
If the authorizations were decided or canceled due to moving out, notification of the authorization 
of the change will be sent to the relevant market participants. 
If the datahub operator has concluded a sales contract, the contract to the seller 
a notification of the termination of the contract is sent. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The wrong contract is concluded → The distribution system operator may cut off the electricity from the wrong one 
from the place of use and error correction is required 
Cancellation terms 
The notification must be canceled no later than the end date

6.8 
DH-333 Notice of termination of online contract 
BOARDKKO 363636 DESCRIPTION OF THE NOTIFICATION OF THE TERMINATION OF THE ONLINE AGREEMENT 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution network operator notifies datahub of the termination of the network contract. Also 
the datahub operator can, if necessary, use the event network contract 
for deciding. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution system operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution network operator terminates the network contract when the customer informs them of moving out 
For the Distribution System Operator, the Distribution System Operator terminates the network contract when it is 
received a notification from datahub that the Seller is terminating the corresponding sales contract or 
Otherwise, the distribution network operator will terminate the network contract. 
Information to be reported 
The date of termination of the contract and the reason for the termination of the contract (emigration, 
termination, dismantling, meter removal), billing address for the final bill. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator 
Code 
The place of use can be found in the data hub, belongs to the measurement area and has not been deleted in the space 
disabled or removed from the system. 
The agreement can be found in the datahub at the indicated place of use and is valid until the indicated date 
at the time of termination. 
If the place of use has already been notified of meter removal, a new meter removal is not possible 
inform. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
Reason "Moving out" or "Dismantling": Current day - 90 days ahead. 
Reason "Termination": 14 - 90 days ahead. 
Reason "Remove meter": Back one month - current day. 
If the reason is "moving out" and the event is a response to the DH-331 sales contract 
termination, the termination date of the online contract must be the same as the corresponding one 
the end date of the sales contract. In this case, an online contract 
deviating from the normal time limits, the decision is also allowed for the past day.   
Processing 
If the place of use does not have a new online contract starting immediately after the expiring online contract, everything 
authorizations that are valid at the time of termination at the place of use or that come into force after that are terminated 
until the end of the contract or canceled in the case of future authorizations. If the place of use has 
starting a new online agreement immediately after the expiring online agreement, authorizations that are valid 
at the end of the agreement or come into force after that is decided at the time of the end of the agreement or 
will be canceled if the customer of the authorization is not also a customer with a new online contract. Authorizations 
will be canceled if the authorization is not still valid at the time of termination.

6.9 
DH-340 Cancellation of contract 
6.9.1 
DH-341 Notice of cancellation of the sales contract 
TABLE 373737 DESCRIPTION OF THE NOTICE OF CANCELLATION OF THE SALES AGREEMENT 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller announces the cancellation of the sales contract at the place of use. Also datahub 
if necessary, the operator can use the transaction to cancel the sales contract. 
Parties and roles 
New seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution network operator (Network service provider), 
Previous Seller (Seller) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The customer informs the seller that he is canceling the sales contract in accordance with the law 
based on their right of cancellation, or the seller or the customer discovers that the information has been declared incorrectly 
of the sales contract, or the seller receives information about the cancellation of the online contract. 
Information to be reported 
ID of the place of use, contract ID, start date of the contract to be canceled, 
possible explanation of the reason for cancellation, reason code for cancellation (Customer cancelled 
of the contract, the Seller canceled the contract, the Distribution System Operator canceled 
agreement or the Customer canceled the agreement but no move-in). 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The contract to be canceled belongs to the notifying seller. 
Code 
The place of use must be found in the data hub and its status must not be "Removedof use' or 
"Removed from the system". 
The contract to be canceled can be found in datahub, the effective date of the cancellation is indicated 
corresponds to the beginning of the contract and the contract is valid at the time of cancellation. 
The contract to be canceled either does not have an end time in the data hub, or it does 
the end time is in the future. 
If the cancellation reason code is "The customer canceled the contract but no 
move-in', the reason for the contract to be canceled must be move-in. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The customer's cancellation can be reported no more than one year back. Seller's or 
the cancellation of the distribution system operator can be notified no more than 10 years back. 
Cancellation of the sales contract can be notified no earlier than 90 days 
in advance. 
Processing 
Balance sheet information 
The contract and balance sheet information of the place of use is registered in the document "Sähkön 
retail market business processes" in accordance with chapter 3.2.5.1. 
Unconfirmed 
network contract 
cancellation 
If the distribution system operator has not yet confirmed the sales contract to be cancelled 
corresponding online contract, the system cancels the unconfirmed one 
network contract automatically. 
Authorizations 
return 
If customer authorizations have been decided when creating the contract to be canceled, they 
shall be reinstated in connection with the reinstatement of the sales contract.

from termination to data hub.

in a later version update. 
TABLE 404040 DESCRIPTION OF THE TERMINATION OF THE ONLINE AGREEMENT IN THE SITUATION OF CANCELLATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator announces the termination of the network contract in the cancellation process 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator decides on its own network contract received from the seller 
based on message DH-343-2  
Information to be reported 
The information corresponding to the contract termination notice DH-333 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The returned contract to be terminated belongs to the reporting distribution system operator. 
Code 
The place of use can be found in the data hub, the place of use belongs to the measurement area and is not in the space 
“disabled” or “removed from the system”. 
The contract to be concluded can be found in datahub, is related to the indicated place of use and is 
valid at the stated end time. 
The reason for the termination of the contract must be termination. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
To be sent no later than the next business day after the DH-343-2 is received  
from the message. The end date can be the current day at the earliest and the 90th at the most 
a day away in the future. 
Processing 
If the place of use does not have a new online contract starting immediately after the expiring online contract, everything 
authorizations that are valid at the time of termination at the place of use or that come into force after that are terminated 
until the end of the contract or canceled in the case of future authorizations. If the place of use has 
starting a new online agreement immediately after the expiring online agreement, authorizations that are valid 
at the end of the agreement or come into force after that is decided at the time of the end of the agreement or 
will be canceled if the customer of the authorization is not also a customer with a new online contract. Authorizations 
will be canceled if the authorization is not still valid at the time of termination. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
Datahub stores the termination information of the online contract 
Processed data 
Possible changes to authorizations. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Information about successful notification receipt or notification rejection.

6.10 
DH-351 Cancellation of termination of sales contract 
TABLE 414141 DESCRIPTION OF THE CANCELLATION OF THE SALE AGREEMENT 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller informs datahub of the cancellation of the end of the sales contract 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution Network Operator (Network Service Provider), 3rd party 
(Energy service provider). 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller cancels the termination of the sales contract with the information he received from the customer 
basis or because the decision was made incorrectly. 
Information to be reported 
End date of the contract to be canceled, reason for the end of the contract 
(moving out, canceling the contract, terminating the contract, the seller's actions 
end), contract information, place of use, measurement area and optional legend. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The contract belongs to the notifying seller. 
Code 
The access point can be found in the data hub and is not in the state "disabled" or "deleted 
from the system". 
The stated place of use has a sales contract that is about to expire DH-331 
as a result of the event and has the same contract ID, the same end date and 
the same reason for termination as in the cancellation notice. 
The location of use does not have a new contract starting after the end date. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The original contract end date is tomorrow or later 
in the future. 
Processing 
If the original termination of the contract caused the cancellation of the future sales contract (DH-331-5), 
the canceled contract is reinstated. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
The termination of the contract corresponding to the notice is cancelled. The sales contract continues 
as it was, just without the canceled ending. If canceled DH-331 
event updated the billing address of the contract, the previous billing address is returned 
into force. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Information about a successful transaction or notification rejection. If cancellation 
is rejected because the place of use has a new contract starting after the end date, 
the start date of the new contract is returned. 
Transmission of information 
The cancellation is forwarded to the distribution system operator, if by agreement, the termination of which 
is cancelled, customers with a corresponding network contract are the same as the original 
end date.

If the cancellation of the termination is a response to an initiation by the distribution system operator 
to the contract termination cancellation process, a notice of cancellation will also be forwarded 
in this case to the distribution system operator.  
If the original termination of the contract was forwarded to a parallel place of use 
to the seller, the cancellation is forwarded to the same seller. Only the reason for the termination of the contract, 
the end date, legend, place of use code and measurement area are forwarded. 
The ID of the seller who reported the cancellation is not forwarded. 
If the original termination of the contract was forwarded to third parties, 
the cancellation is forwarded to the same third parties. The notification contains the same information, 
which are forwarded to the seller of the parallel access point. 
If the original pthe conclusion of the lesson caused a future contract 
of cancellation, information about the reinstatement of the agreement will be forwarded to the returned 
to the seller of the sales contract. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Termination of the wrong contract is canceled → May cause retroactive corrections 
later.

Can't cancel.

7.1 
DH-411 Delivery connection request 
TABLE 434343 DESCRIPTION OF THE SELLER'S DELIVERY CONNECTION REQUEST 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller informs the datahub of the connection request for delivery of the point of use 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller requests connection of the delivery from the distribution system operator when 
• 
the customer pays the overdue invoice or fixes something else 
breach of contract 
• 
the seller cancels the disconnection request on the requested disconnection date 
Information to be reported 
Connection date, usage location status (="connected"), usage location ID, 
connection contact information 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have a valid sales contract for the place of use of the request 
at the time of notification and the date of connection. 
Code 
The access point is not in the state "disabled" or "removed from the system". 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The effective time of the connection request is the current day or a maximum of 90 days 
in the future. 
Processing 
If there is an open connection or disconnection request from the seller at the same point of use, whose connection/disconnection date is 
in the past, the previous request is closed in the system so that it is no longer waited for 
response from the distribution system operator.  
If the seller announces the connection request for the same day that the seller has previously announced 
disconnection request, the balance sheet information of the seller that ended in connection with the disconnection request is attached back to the seller. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding

7.2 
DH-412 Notice of connection of delivery 
TABLE 444444 DESCRIPTION OF THE DISTRIBUTION NETWORK OPERATOR'S SUPPLY CONNECTION NOTIFICATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator will notify the electricity connection of the place of use that has taken place 
to datahub. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator switches on the electricity at the point of use, for example, when 
• 
A move-in will be made to the discontinued/vendor-less place of use 
• 
the renovation work at the site of use will be completed 
• 
the customer pays the outstanding distribution system operator's invoice 
• 
the customer requests electricity connection from the distribution system operator 
• 
the seller has requested to connect the electricity to the place of use (DH-411) 
Information to be reported 
Time of connection to the time step of the measurement of the place of use (hour or 15 minutes) 
with accuracy (15 minutes from the introduction of the balance sheet, one hour before that 
accuracy), connection status of the user location (="connected"), user location ID 
Validation 
 
Rights to information 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator. 
Code 
The status of the place of use is not "disabled". 
The connection date must not be in the future. 
Mandatory attributes of usage location properties must have values. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
If the place of use is in the state "disconnected" at the request of the seller (DH-421), this will appear 
the notification is preceded by the seller's request for connection (DH-411). 
Time limits 
The connection must be reported to the datahub immediately after the connection when the information is available 
available from the distribution system operator's system. If there is no information, for example 
of manually connected targets are not available immediately after the connection has been completed, 
even in these cases, the notification must be sent to the datahub after one week at the latest 
from when the customer's electricity supply is connected, when the customer's annual estimate is less than 1 
GWh and at the latest on the working day following connection, in the case of 1 GWh or 
a customer who spends more per year. Information about the connection is still being received 
even after the time, but notifications sent repeatedly late are received 
to intervene. 
Processing 
 
The balance information of the place of use is attached, according to the time step of the measurement, to the notification to the seller of the place of use 
from the hour or quarter of the moment of connection, if the balance information has previously been decided in the seller's disconnection request (DH-
421) starting from the day following the announced disconnection date and the seller has notified a connection request (DH-
411) before the connection notification described in this table. The balance sheet is attached to the seller upon connection 
also without the seller's connection request, if the previous disconnection has not taken place at the seller's request. Balance sheet information 
however, a maximum of au of the balance window is always connectedfor the specified period, if the connection notification is made earlier than this 
for time.

Event description 
Definition

has been requested for the wrong operating location or there is no longer a need to connect the operating location.

Validation 
 
Rights to information

at the time of transmission and on the cancelable connection date. 
Code 
The point of use has a pending connection request from the same vendor for the same date 
(the connection date of the cancellation corresponds to the originally requested connection date). 
The connection request is considered pending as long as the distribution system operator is not present 
sent a DH-412 transaction, delay notices do not affect the situation. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The effective date cannot be in the past. 
Processing

connection notification of the distribution system operator.

for the connection request

7.4 
DH-421 Delivery Interruption Request 
TABLE 464646 DESCRIPTION OF THE SELLER'S DELIVERY INTERRUPTION REQUEST 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller informs the datahub of the request to interrupt the delivery of the place of use 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller), Datahub, Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller requests the interruption of delivery from the distribution system operator when 
• 
the customer fails to pay the seller's invoices or is guilty of something else 
breach of contract 
Information to be reported 
Disconnection date, location status (="disconnected"), location ID 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The seller must have a valid sales contract for the place of use of the request 
at the time of notification and the date of disconnection. 
Code 
The place of use is not in the state "disabled" 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The request must be submitted no later than one week before the desired cut-off date 
Processing 
The electricity consumption of the place of use is calculated from the day after the requested cut-off date 
to the balance sheet of the distribution network operator (electricity consumption is counted again in the seller's balance sheet of the connection notice 
DH-412 after switching on). 
If there is an open connection or disconnection request from the seller at the same point of use, whose connection/disconnection date is 
in the past, the previous request is closed in the system so that it is no longer waited for 
response from the distribution system operator. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
Balance sheet of the place of use 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of a successful or rejected disconnection request 
Transmission of information 
The disconnection request is forwarded to the distribution network operator of the place of use 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
The disconnection request is reported to the wrong place of use or the wrong day → 
the distribution system operator interrupts the customer's supply on the wrong grounds (consequences 
correspond to a sudden power cut) 
Cancellation terms 
The cancellation must be made before the notification of the distribution system operator in section 7.5, but 
no later than the day before the requested cut-off date. On the cut-off day 
the process can be canceled by reporting a connection request (DH-411).

TABLE 474747 DESCRIPTION OF DISTRIBUTION NETWORK OPERATOR'S NOTIFICATION OF SUPPLY INTERRUPTION  
Event description 
Definition

to datahub. 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator (Network service provider), Datahub, Seller (Seller) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator cuts off the electricity at the point of use, for example, when 
• 
the place of use is without a seller 
• 
renovation works are carried out at the site of use 
• 
the customer leaves the distribution system operator's invoices unpaid 
• 
the customer requests a power cut from the distribution network operator 
• 
the seller requests a power cut (DH-421) 
Information to be reported 
The moment of disconnection to the time step of the measurement of the place of use (one hour or 15 minutes) 
with accuracy (15 minutes from the introduction of the balance sheet, one hour before that 
accuracy), connection status of the operating location (="switched off"), ID of the operating location. If 
the distribution system operator informs that the disconnection requested by the seller will not be carried out by the seller 
due to the connection request you indicated for the same day (cancellation of the disconnection request 
on the day of disconnection), the connection status is reported as "connected". 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use belongs to the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator. 
Code 
The status of the place of use is not "disabled". 
The cut-off date must not be in the future. 
Mandatory attributes of usage location properties must have values. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The disconnection must be reported to datahub immediately after the disconnection when the information is available 
available from the distribution system operator's system. If there is no information, for example 
of targets that can be disconnected manually, not immediately after the completed disconnection 
available, the Notification must also be sent to datahub in these cases at the latest 
a week after the customer's electricity supply has been cut off, when the customer 
the annual estimate is less than 1 GWh and at the latest on the working day following the disconnection, when 
this is a customer using 1 GWh or more per year. Information about disconnection 
are still accepted after this time, but repeatedly late 
notifications sent will be addressed.

-

Event description 
Definition

with the date. 
Parties and roles

Event launch 
Starts when

on the appropriate day. 
Information to be reported 
Location ID; A possible reason why the requested operation is not successful 
date or information that the procedure cannot be performed at all 
to the place of use; Possible date when the procedure can be done at the earliest 
succeed. 
Validation 
Rights to information

The seller must have a valid contract for the place of use 
Code 
- 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
The original request must not include the notification of section 7.2 
Time limits 
No later than the business day following the connection date requested by the seller, if 
7.2 notification has not yet been made for the request in question. Notification will be taken 
I will still reply even after this time, but repeatedly to those sent late 
notifications will be addressed.

-

- 
Processed data 
-
