TABLE 505050 DESCRIPTION OF INTERRUPTION DELAY NOTIFICATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The distribution system operator responds to the seller's disconnection request that the operation is not successful 
on the requested date 
Parties and roles 
Distribution network operator, Datahub, (Seller) 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The distribution system operator is unable to carry out the disconnection on the day requested by the seller 
Information to be reported 
Location ID; A possible reason why the requested operation is not successful 
date or information that the procedure cannot be performed at all 
to the place of use; Possible date when the procedure can be successful at the earliest. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The place of use must be in the measurement area of ​​the distribution system operator 
The seller must have a valid contract for the place of use 
Code 
- 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
The original request must not include the notification of section 7.5 
Time limits 
No later than the business day following the cut-off date requested by the seller, if 7.5 
notification has not yet been made for the request in question. Notification is accepted 
even after this time, but for notifications sent repeatedly late 
will be addressed. 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
- 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Notification of successful or rejected notification 
Transmission of information 
The information provided by the distribution system operator is forwarded to the seller who sent the request. 
The forwarded request must contain a reference to the original request. 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
-

8 
DH-500-Balance statement 
 
FIGURE 525252 BALANCE SHEET SETTLEMENT EVENTS 
Datahub performs balance settlement calculations for distribution system operators and delivers 
balance sheet information for eSett. Data transmission takes place in accordance with NBS specifications (www.ediel.org), 
and events related to information exchange are not described in this document. 
eSett delivers distribution network operators' balance deviation information and confirmed limit point sumsto datahub and datahub forwards the information to distribution system operators and sellers. Also datahub and eSett 
the events between follow the NBS specifications (www.ediel.org) and are not described here 
in the document.

10.1 
DH-711, DH-712 Product creation  
TABLE 646464 DESCRIPTION FOR PRODUCT CREATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or distribution system operator reports their own product information to the data hub 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller/Distribution system operator creates a new product 
Information to be reported 
Party ID; product information and product component information. 
If the product has a component whose price information type is "BG01=Fixed price", 
must also deliver the component price information with process DH-713 or DH-714 product 
to activate. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
- 
Code 
The party must provide all structural information of the product at once. 
A combination of product ID and component ID and product ID 
must be individual. 
The languages ​​of the product and product components must match. If the product has 
English name, each component of the product must also have 
English name. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The earliest is the current day and no more than 90 days in the future. 
Processing 
If the created product has a component whose price information type is "BG01=Fixed price", the creation process remains 
to wait for price information for the component before activating it. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
Product information and product component information. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Acceptance or rejection of information 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Product information is reported incorrectly → the automated invoicing process may produce incorrect information 
invoices or incorrect information may be given to the customer 
Cancellation terms 
The product creation can be canceled by informing the product of the same end date 
than the previously announced start date.

10.2 
DH-713, DH-714 Price information update 
TABLE 656565 DESCRIPTION OF UPDATE OF PRICE INFORMATION 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or distribution system operator updates the prices of their products. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller/Distribution system operator will notify the change in the price of the product. 
The seller/Distribution system operator creates a new price information for a product that has at least one 
a component with price data type BG01. 
Information to be reported 
Product owner; product, product component, price, price start time. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The parties can only update their own product information 
Code 
Only future prices are announced. 
Only one price can be valida at some point in time. 
The price can only be declared for a product that has not expired when the price takes effect. 
The prices are valid for whole days. 
Only one price can be declared at a time. 
The end time of the price cannot be set with this event. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
30 – 365 days into the future. (When creating a new product, the starting time of the price must be 
same as the start time of the product, then this time limit does not apply.) 
Processing 
The end time of the price is automatically set to match the end time of the product in transaction DH-717/718. 
Announcing the end of the price will cause an error in validation. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
The declared price is saved. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Acceptance or rejection of information. 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Product information is reported incorrectly → the automated invoicing process may produce incorrect information 
invoices or incorrect information may be given to the customer 
Cancellation terms 
Future prices can be corrected by announcing new information at the same start time when 
existing data will be overwritten. If there are prices before the time limit of the event 
need to change, it can be done by the datahub operator.

DH-715, DH-716 Price time series or calendar time series update 
TABLE 666666 DESCRIPTION OF PRICE TIME SERIES OR CALENDAR TIME SERIES UPDATE 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or the distribution system operator announces changes to the price time series or 
to the calendar time series. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The seller/Distribution system operator announces changes to the price time series or 
to the calendar time series. 
Information to be reported 
Product owner, product, product component, price, price validity period. 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The parties can only update their own product information 
Code 
Price time series can be reported retrospectively. 
Only one price time series can be valid at any given time. 
The start time of the price time series must correspond to the start time of the product at the time of creation or it 
must correspond to the end time of the previous one. 
When updating an existing price-time series, it should match the previous one 
the indicated period of the price time series. 
The end time of the calendar or price time series must not exceed the end time of the product. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
-365 – 365 days from the moment of notification. 
The calendar time series must be announced by the end of September at the latest 
for the coming year. 
Processing 
- 
Data storage 
Reported information 
The reported time series data is saved. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Acceptance or rejection of information. 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Product information is reported incorrectly → the automated invoicing process may produce incorrect information 
invoices or incorrect information may be given to the customer 
Cancellation terms 
Price time series can be corrected by announcing new data in the same time period, 
in which case the existing data will be overwritten.

10.4 
DH-717, DH-718 Product structural information update 
TABLE 676767 DESCRIPTION OF PRODUCT STRUCTURAL INFORMATION UPDATE 
Event description 
Definition 
The seller or distribution network operator notifies of changes to the product information. 
Parties and roles 
Seller (Seller) / Distribution System Operator (Network Service Provider), Datahub 
Event initiation 
Starts when 
Seller/Distribution System Operator reports a change to product information. 
Information to be reported 
Party ID; product name, product component name or product end date. 
Validation 
Data rights 
Parties can only update their own product information 
Rules 
Only changes to product description, end date, product name (including 
language information) and product component name (including 
language information) and 
tax rate are allowed. This includes deleting product or product component 
name data sets, as long as at least 
one name data remains for both the product and the product component. 
Interrupting 
Events 
- 
Time limits 
Current day – 90 days into the future. 
If the end date of a product is updated, the end date can be no earlier than 30 days 
from the update time (unless the product is canceled, in which case the end date is the product start date). 
Processing 
If the end date of a product is updated, the end date is updated for product components and prices. 
Data storage 
Reported data 
Product data and product component data. Old data is overwritten. 
Processed data 
- 
Data return/forwarding 
Data return 
Data acceptance or rejection. 
Data forwarding 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors and 
consequences 
Product data is reported incorrectly → the automated invoicing process may produce incorrect 
invoices or the customer may be given incorrect information 
Cancellation conditions 
Data will be corrected with a new update.

IMAGE 767676 AUTHORIZATION EVENTS 
11.1 
DH-811, DH-812, DH-813 Notification of the customer's authorization 
from the party 
TABLE 727272 DESCRIPTION OF PARTY-PARTY CUSTOMER AUTHORIZATION NOTIFICATION 
Event description 
Definition 
A seller, distribution system operator or other 3rd party registered in Datahub requests the right 
to the customer's information 
Parties and roles 
Seller/Distribution system operator/3rd party (Energy service provider), Datahub 
Event launch 
Starts when 
The party has a business need and the customer's authorization to obtain the right 
to the customer's information in datahub 
Information to be reported 
Unique identifiers of customers who have given authorization; its place of use 
the ID to which the authorization has been issued1; the date from which the authorization begins; date, 
when the authorization ends; the purpose of the authorization (list) and a voluntary explanation 
Validation 
Rights to information 
The party must be registered with datahub. 
The reported customers are business customers. 
Code 
The reported customers and the place of use can be found in datahub. 
The access point is not in the state "Removed" or "Disabled". 
 
1 The authorization cannot be notified to all the customer's places of use without identifying abuses 
to prevent Such an authorization need can be taken care of in the document "Electricity retail market 
business processes in datahub" through the service described in chapter 3.11.

7 November 2023 
 
 
 
 
 
  
 
382 (468) 
 
Fingrid Datahub Oy 
Street address 
Postal address

Läkkisepäntie 21

If the reported customers do not have contracts related to the authorization information 
at the place of use for the entire validity period of the authorization, authorization cannot be granted 
indicate with the authorization type Energy reporting (the customer has a contract for the place of use), 
Request for quotation (the customer has a contract for the place of use) or tendering for the contract 
as a service (the customer has a contract for the place of use). 
If the authorization valid at the time of notification is updated, the authorization 
the start date cannot be changed.  
The seller (DH-811) can notify the authorization with the following purposes: 
• 
Request for quotation (the customer has a contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer has the contract for the place of use) 
• 
Request for quotation (the customer does not have a contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer does not have a contract for the place of use) 
The 3rd party (DH-812) can notify the authorization with the following purposes: 
• 
Energy reporting (customera contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer has the contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer does not have a contract for the place of use) 
The distribution network operator (DH-813) cannot report the authorization in any way (currently 
in use) on purpose. 
Interrupting 
proceedings 
- 
Time limits 
The start time must not be in the past or more than 90 days in the future. 
The maximum period of validity of the authorization is: 
• 
2 business days "Request for quotation" with authorization reason 
• 
30 days with "Contract tendering as a service" authorization reason 
• 
2 years "Energy reporting" for authorization reason 
Processing 
If an authorization already exists for the same party, customer, place of use and purpose 
authorization information, the newly reported authorization information is saved on top of the previously reported authorization information 
to replace the previous authorization.  
If several customers are associated with the reported authorization information, datahub stores the authorization information individually 
per customer and location of use. 
Data storage 
Reported information 
Storage of authorization information 
Processed data 
If more than one customer is associated with the declared authorization information, save datahub 
authorization information separately for each customer and place of use. 
Data return/forwarding 
Data recovery 
Acknowledgment of acceptance/rejection of the notification. 
Transmission of information 
- 
Errors and cancellations 
Significant errors 
and consequences 
The authorization is reported to the wrong places of use → the party receives information that it does not have 
right. The party must cancel the authorization and dispose of the information that it has already received 
apply from datahub

Energy reporting (the customer has a contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer has the contract for the place of use) 
• 
Tendering of the contract as a service (the customer does not have a contract 
to the place of use) 
The distribution system operator (DH-823) is not allowed to be authorized in any way (currently 
in use) on purpose.
